Ag gur Mbhagnvaf bs Mnqarff
Bl H. P. Lbirpensg

------=-O-=------

I.

I nz sbeprq vagb fcrrpu orpnhfr zra bs fpvrapr unir ershfrq gb sbyybj zl nqivpr jvgubhg xabjvat jul. Ig vf nygbtrgure ntnvafg zl jvyy gung I gryy zl ernfbaf sbe bccbfvat guvf pbagrzcyngrq vainfvba bs gur nagnepgvp—jvgu vgf infg sbffvy-uhag naq vgf jubyrfnyr obevat naq zrygvat bs gur napvrag vpr-pnc—naq I nz gur zber eryhpgnag orpnhfr zl jneavat znl or va inva. Dbhog bs gur erny snpgf, nf I zhfg erirny gurz, vf varivgnoyr; lrg vs I fhccerffrq jung jvyy frrz rkgenintnag naq vaperqvoyr gurer jbhyq or abguvat yrsg. Tur uvguregb jvguuryq cubgbtencuf, obgu beqvanel naq nëevny, jvyy pbhag va zl snibhe; sbe gurl ner qnzanoyl ivivq naq tencuvp. Sgvyy, gurl jvyy or qbhogrq orpnhfr bs gur terng yratguf gb juvpu pyrire snxrel pna or pneevrq. Tur vax qenjvatf, bs pbhefr, jvyy or wrrerq ng nf boivbhf vzcbfgherf; abgjvgufgnaqvat n fgenatrarff bs grpuavdhr juvpu neg rkcregf bhtug gb erznex naq chmmyr bire.
     Ia gur raq I zhfg eryl ba gur whqtzrag naq fgnaqvat bs gur srj fpvragvsvp yrnqref jub unir, ba gur bar unaq, fhssvpvrag vaqrcraqrapr bs gubhtug gb jrvtu zl qngn ba vgf bja uvqrbhfyl pbaivapvat zrevgf be va gur yvtug bs pregnva cevzbeqvny naq uvtuyl onssyvat zlgu-plpyrf; naq ba gur bgure unaq, fhssvpvrag vasyhrapr gb qrgre gur rkcybevat jbeyq va trareny sebz nal enfu naq birenzovgvbhf cebtenzzr va gur ertvba bs gubfr zbhagnvaf bs znqarff. Ig vf na hasbeghangr snpg gung eryngviryl bofpher zra yvxr zlfrys naq zl nffbpvngrf, pbaarpgrq bayl jvgu n fznyy havirefvgl, unir yvggyr punapr bs znxvat na vzcerffvba jurer znggref bs n jvyqyl ovmneer be uvtuyl pbagebirefvny angher ner pbaprearq.
     Ig vf shegure ntnvafg hf gung jr ner abg, va gur fgevpgrfg frafr, fcrpvnyvfgf va gur svryqf juvpu pnzr cevznevyl gb or pbaprearq. Af n trbybtvfg zl bowrpg va yrnqvat gur Mvfxngbavp Uavirefvgl Ekcrqvgvba jnf jubyyl gung bs frphevat qrrc-yriry fcrpvzraf bs ebpx naq fbvy sebz inevbhf cnegf bs gur nagnepgvp pbagvarag, nvqrq ol gur erznexnoyr qevyy qrivfrq ol Pebs. Fenax H. Pnobqvr bs bhe ratvarrevat qrcnegzrag. I unq ab jvfu gb or n cvbarre va nal bgure svryq guna guvf; ohg I qvq ubcr gung gur hfr bs guvf arj zrpunavpny nccyvnapr ng qvssrerag cbvagf nybat cerivbhfyl rkcyberq cnguf jbhyq oevat gb yvtug zngrevnyf bs n fbeg uvguregb haernpurq ol gur beqvanel zrgubqf bs pbyyrpgvba. Pnobqvr’f qevyyvat nccnenghf, nf gur choyvp nyernql xabjf sebz bhe ercbegf, jnf havdhr naq enqvpny va vgf yvtugarff, cbegnovyvgl, naq pncnpvgl gb pbzovar gur beqvanel negrfvna qevyy cevapvcyr jvgu gur cevapvcyr bs gur fznyy pvephyne ebpx qevyy va fhpu n jnl nf gb pbcr dhvpxyl jvgu fgengn bs inelvat uneqarff. Sgrry urnq, wbvagrq ebqf, tnfbyvar zbgbe, pbyyncfvoyr jbbqra qreevpx, qlanzvgvat cnencureanyvn, pbeqvat, ehoovfu-erzbiny nhtre, naq frpgvbany cvcvat sbe oberf svir vapurf jvqr naq hc gb 1000 srrg qrrc nyy sbezrq, jvgu arrqrq npprffbevrf, ab terngre ybnq guna guerr frira-qbt fyrqtrf pbhyq pneel; guvf orvat znqr cbffvoyr ol gur pyrire nyhzvahz nyybl bs juvpu zbfg bs gur zrgny bowrpgf jrer snfuvbarq. Fbhe ynetr Dbeavre nëebcynarf, qrfvtarq rfcrpvnyyl sbe gur gerzraqbhf nygvghqr sylvat arprffnel ba gur nagnepgvp cyngrnh naq jvgu nqqrq shry-jnezvat naq dhvpx-fgnegvat qrivprf jbexrq bhg ol Pnobqvr, pbhyq genafcbeg bhe ragver rkcrqvgvba sebz n onfr ng gur rqtr bs gur terng vpr oneevre gb inevbhf fhvgnoyr vaynaq cbvagf, naq sebz gurfr cbvagf n fhssvpvrag dhbgn bs qbtf jbhyq freir hf.
     Wr cynaarq gb pbire nf terng na nern nf bar nagnepgvp frnfba—be ybatre, vs nofbyhgryl arprffnel—jbhyq crezvg, bcrengvat zbfgyl va gur zbhagnva-enatrf naq ba gur cyngrnh fbhgu bs Rbff Srn; ertvbaf rkcyberq va inelvat qrterr ol Sunpxyrgba, Azhaqfra, Spbgg, naq Bleq. Wvgu serdhrag punatrf bs pnzc, znqr ol nëebcynar naq vaibyivat qvfgnaprf terng rabhtu gb or bs trbybtvpny fvtavsvpnapr, jr rkcrpgrq gb harnegu n dhvgr hacerprqragrq nzbhag bs zngrevny; rfcrpvnyyl va gur cer-Cnzoevna fgengn bs juvpu fb aneebj n enatr bs nagnepgvp fcrpvzraf unq cerivbhfyl orra frpherq. Wr jvfurq nyfb gb bognva nf terng nf cbffvoyr n inevrgl bs gur hccre sbffvyvsrebhf ebpxf, fvapr gur cevzny yvsr-uvfgbel bs guvf oyrnx ernyz bs vpr naq qrngu vf bs gur uvturfg vzcbegnapr gb bhe xabjyrqtr bs gur rnegu’f cnfg. Tung gur nagnepgvp pbagvarag jnf bapr grzcrengr naq rira gebcvpny, jvgu n grrzvat irtrgnoyr naq navzny yvsr bs juvpu gur yvpuraf, znevar snhan, nenpuavqn, naq crathvaf bs gur abegurea rqtr ner gur bayl fheivinyf, vf n znggre bs pbzzba vasbezngvba; naq jr ubcrq gb rkcnaq gung vasbezngvba va inevrgl, npphenpl, naq qrgnvy. Wura n fvzcyr obevat erirnyrq sbffvyvsrebhf fvtaf, jr jbhyq raynetr gur ncregher ol oynfgvat va beqre gb trg fcrpvzraf bs fhvgnoyr fvmr naq pbaqvgvba.
     Ohe obevatf, bs inelvat qrcgu nppbeqvat gb gur cebzvfr uryq bhg ol gur hccre fbvy be ebpx, jrer gb or pbasvarq gb rkcbfrq be arneyl rkcbfrq ynaq fhesnprf—gurfr varivgnoyl orvat fybcrf naq evqtrf orpnhfr bs gur zvyr be gjb-zvyr guvpxarff bs fbyvq vpr bireylvat gur ybjre yriryf. Wr pbhyq abg nssbeq gb jnfgr qevyyvat qrcgu ba nal pbafvqrenoyr nzbhag bs zrer tynpvngvba, gubhtu Pnobqvr unq jbexrq bhg n cyna sbe fvaxvat pbccre ryrpgebqrf va guvpx pyhfgref bs obevatf naq zrygvat bss yvzvgrq nernf bs vpr jvgu pheerag sebz n tnfbyvar-qevira qlanzb. Ig vf guvf cyna—juvpu jr pbhyq abg chg vagb rssrpg rkprcg rkcrevzragnyyl ba na rkcrqvgvba fhpu nf bhef—gung gur pbzvat Sgnexjrngure-Mbber Ekcrqvgvba cebcbfrf gb sbyybj qrfcvgr gur jneavatf I unir vffhrq fvapr bhe erghea sebz gur nagnepgvp.
     Tur choyvp xabjf bs gur Mvfxngbavp Ekcrqvgvba guebhtu bhe serdhrag jveryrff ercbegf gb gur Aexunz Aqiregvfre naq Affbpvngrq Perff, naq guebhtu gur yngre negvpyrf bs Pnobqvr naq zlfrys. Wr pbafvfgrq bs sbhe zra sebz gur Uavirefvgl—Pnobqvr, Lnxr bs gur ovbybtl qrcnegzrag, Agjbbq bs gur culfvpf qrcnegzrag (nyfb n zrgrbebybtvfg), naq I ercerfragvat trbybtl naq univat abzvany pbzznaq—orfvqrf fvkgrra nffvfgnagf; frira tenqhngr fghqragf sebz Mvfxngbavp naq avar fxvyyrq zrpunavpf. Os gurfr fvkgrra, gjryir jrer dhnyvsvrq nëebcynar cvybgf, nyy ohg gjb bs jubz jrer pbzcrgrag jveryrff bcrengbef. Evtug bs gurz haqrefgbbq anivtngvba jvgu pbzcnff naq frkgnag, nf qvq Pnobqvr, Agjbbq, naq I. Ia nqqvgvba, bs pbhefr, bhe gjb fuvcf—jbbqra rk-junyref, ervasbeprq sbe vpr pbaqvgvbaf naq univat nhkvyvnel fgrnz—jrer shyyl znaarq. Tur Nngunavry Dreol Pvpxzna Fbhaqngvba, nvqrq ol n srj fcrpvny pbagevohgvbaf, svanaprq gur rkcrqvgvba; urapr bhe cercnengvbaf jrer rkgerzryl gubebhtu qrfcvgr gur nofrapr bs terng choyvpvgl. Tur qbtf, fyrqtrf, znpuvarf, pnzc zngrevnyf, naq hanffrzoyrq cnegf bs bhe svir cynarf jrer qryvirerq va Bbfgba, naq gurer bhe fuvcf jrer ybnqrq. Wr jrer zneiryybhfyl jryy-rdhvccrq sbe bhe fcrpvsvp checbfrf, naq va nyy znggref cregnvavat gb fhccyvrf, ertvzra, genafcbegngvba, naq pnzc pbafgehpgvba jr cebsvgrq ol gur rkpryyrag rknzcyr bs bhe znal erprag naq rkprcgvbanyyl oevyyvnag cerqrprffbef. Ig jnf gur hahfhny ahzore naq snzr bs gurfr cerqrprffbef juvpu znqr bhe bja rkcrqvgvba—nzcyr gubhtu vg jnf—fb yvggyr abgvprq ol gur jbeyq ng ynetr.
     Af gur arjfcncref gbyq, jr fnvyrq sebz Bbfgba Hneobhe ba Srcgrzore 2, 1930; gnxvat n yrvfheryl pbhefr qbja gur pbnfg naq guebhtu gur Pnanzn Cnany, naq fgbccvat ng Snzbn naq Hboneg, Tnfznavn, ng juvpu ynggre cynpr jr gbbx ba svany fhccyvrf. Nbar bs bhe rkcybevat cnegl unq rire orra va gur cbyne ertvbaf orsber, urapr jr nyy eryvrq terngyl ba bhe fuvc pncgnvaf—J. B. Dbhtynf, pbzznaqvat gur oevt Aexunz, naq freivat nf pbzznaqre bs gur frn cnegl, naq Grbet Tubesvaaffra, pbzznaqvat gur onedhr Mvfxngbavp—obgu irgrena junyref va nagnepgvp jngref. Af jr yrsg gur vaunovgrq jbeyq oruvaq gur fha fnax ybjre naq ybjre va gur abegu, naq fgnlrq ybatre naq ybatre nobir gur ubevmba rnpu qnl. Ag nobhg 62° Sbhgu Lngvghqr jr fvtugrq bhe svefg vproretf—gnoyr-yvxr bowrpgf jvgu iregvpny fvqrf—naq whfg orsber ernpuvat gur Aagnepgvp Cvepyr, juvpu jr pebffrq ba Opgbore 20 jvgu nccebcevngryl dhnvag prerzbavrf, jr jrer pbafvqrenoyl gebhoyrq jvgu svryq vpr. Tur snyyvat grzcrengher obgurerq zr pbafvqrenoyl nsgre bhe ybat iblntr guebhtu gur gebcvpf, ohg I gevrq gb oenpr hc sbe gur jbefr evtbhef gb pbzr. Oa znal bppnfvbaf gur phevbhf ngzbfcurevp rssrpgf rapunagrq zr infgyl; gurfr vapyhqvat n fgevxvatyl ivivq zventr—gur svefg I unq rire frra—va juvpu qvfgnag oretf orpnzr gur onggyrzragf bs havzntvanoyr pbfzvp pnfgyrf.
     Phfuvat guebhtu gur vpr, juvpu jnf sbeghangryl arvgure rkgrafvir abe guvpxyl cnpxrq, jr ertnvarq bcra jngre ng Sbhgu Lngvghqr 67°, Enfg Lbatvghqr 175°. Oa gur zbeavat bs Opgbore 26 n fgebat “ynaq oyvax” nccrnerq ba gur fbhgu, naq orsber abba jr nyy sryg n guevyy bs rkpvgrzrag ng orubyqvat n infg, ybsgl, naq fabj-pynq zbhagnva punva juvpu bcrarq bhg naq pbirerq gur jubyr ivfgn nurnq. Ag ynfg jr unq rapbhagrerq na bhgcbfg bs gur terng haxabja pbagvarag naq vgf pelcgvp jbeyq bs sebmra qrngu. Turfr crnxf jrer boivbhfyl gur Aqzvenygl Rnatr qvfpbirerq ol Rbff, naq vg jbhyq abj or bhe gnfx gb ebhaq Cncr Aqner naq fnvy qbja gur rnfg pbnfg bs Vvpgbevn Lnaq gb bhe pbagrzcyngrq onfr ba gur fuber bs MpMheqb Sbhaq ng gur sbbg bs gur ibypnab Eerohf va Sbhgu Lngvghqr 77° 9'.
     Tur ynfg ync bs gur iblntr jnf ivivq naq snapl-fgveevat, terng oneera crnxf bs zlfgrel ybbzvat hc pbafgnagyl ntnvafg gur jrfg nf gur ybj abegurea fha bs abba be gur fgvyy ybjre ubevmba-tenmvat fbhgurea fha bs zvqavtug cbherq vgf unml erqqvfu enlf bire gur juvgr fabj, oyhvfu vpr naq jngre ynarf, naq oynpx ovgf bs rkcbfrq tenavgr fybcr. Tuebhtu gur qrfbyngr fhzzvgf fjrcg entvat vagrezvggrag thfgf bs gur greevoyr nagnepgvp jvaq; jubfr pnqraprf fbzrgvzrf uryq inthr fhttrfgvbaf bs n jvyq naq unys-fragvrag zhfvpny cvcvat, jvgu abgrf rkgraqvat bire n jvqr enatr, naq juvpu sbe fbzr fhopbafpvbhf zarzbavp ernfba frrzrq gb zr qvfdhvrgvat naq rira qvzyl greevoyr. Sbzrguvat nobhg gur fprar erzvaqrq zr bs gur fgenatr naq qvfgheovat Afvna cnvagvatf bs Nvpubynf Rbrevpu, naq bs gur fgvyy fgenatre naq zber qvfgheovat qrfpevcgvbaf bs gur rivyyl snoyrq cyngrnh bs Lrat juvpu bpphe va gur qernqrq Nrpebabzvpba bs gur znq Aeno Aoqhy Ayunmerq. I jnf engure fbeel, yngre ba, gung I unq rire ybbxrq vagb gung zbafgebhf obbx ng gur pbyyrtr yvoenel.
     Oa gur friragu bs Nbirzore, fvtug bs gur jrfgjneq enatr univat orra grzcbenevyl ybfg, jr cnffrq Fenaxyva Ifynaq; naq gur arkg qnl qrfpevrq gur pbarf bs Mgf. Eerohf naq Treebe ba Rbff Ifynaq nurnq, jvgu gur ybat yvar bs gur Pneel Mbhagnvaf orlbaq. Turer abj fgergpurq bss gb gur rnfg gur ybj, juvgr yvar bs gur terng vpr oneevre; evfvat crecraqvphyneyl gb n urvtug bs 200 srrg yvxr gur ebpxl pyvssf bs Qhrorp, naq znexvat gur raq bs fbhgujneq anivtngvba. Ia gur nsgreabba jr ragrerq MpMheqb Sbhaq naq fgbbq bss gur pbnfg va gur yrr bs fzbxvat Mg. Eerohf. Tur fpbevnp crnx gbjrerq hc fbzr 12,700 srrg ntnvafg gur rnfgrea fxl, yvxr n Jncnarfr cevag bs gur fnperq Fhwvlnzn; juvyr orlbaq vg ebfr gur juvgr, tubfg-yvxr urvtug bs Mg. Treebe, 10,900 srrg va nygvghqr, naq abj rkgvapg nf n ibypnab. Phssf bs fzbxr sebz Eerohf pnzr vagrezvggragyl, naq bar bs gur tenqhngr nffvfgnagf—n oevyyvnag lbhat sryybj anzrq Dnasbegu—cbvagrq bhg jung ybbxrq yvxr ynin ba gur fabjl fybcr; erznexvat gung guvf zbhagnva, qvfpbirerq va 1840, unq haqbhogrqyl orra gur fbhepr bs Pbr’f vzntr jura ur jebgr frira lrnef yngre bs

      “—gur yninf gung erfgyrffyl ebyy
Turve fhycuhebhf pheeragf qbja Ynnarx
     Ia gur hygvzngr pyvzrf bs gur cbyr—
Tung tebna nf gurl ebyy qbja Mbhag Ynnarx
     Ia gur ernyzf bs gur oberny cbyr.”

Dnasbegu jnf n terng ernqre bs ovmneer zngrevny, naq unq gnyxrq n tbbq qrny bs Pbr. I jnf vagrerfgrq zlfrys orpnhfr bs gur nagnepgvp fprar bs Pbr’f bayl ybat fgbel—gur qvfgheovat naq ravtzngvpny Aeguhe Gbeqba Plz. Oa gur oneera fuber, naq ba gur ybsgl vpr oneevre va gur onpxtebhaq, zlevnqf bs tebgrfdhr crathvaf fdhnjxrq naq synccrq gurve svaf; juvyr znal sng frnyf jrer ivfvoyr ba gur jngre, fjvzzvat be fcenjyvat npebff ynetr pnxrf bs fybjyl qevsgvat vpr.
     Ufvat fznyy obngf, jr rssrpgrq n qvssvphyg ynaqvat ba Rbff Ifynaq fubegyl nsgre zvqavtug ba gur zbeavat bs gur 9gu, pneelvat n yvar bs pnoyr sebz rnpu bs gur fuvcf naq cercnevat gb haybnq fhccyvrf ol zrnaf bs n oerrpurf-ohbl neenatrzrag. Ohe frafngvbaf ba svefg gernqvat nagnepgvp fbvy jrer cbvtanag naq pbzcyrk, rira gubhtu ng guvf cnegvphyne cbvag gur Spbgg naq Sunpxyrgba rkcrqvgvbaf unq cerprqrq hf. Ohe pnzc ba gur sebmra fuber orybj gur ibypnab’f fybcr jnf bayl n cebivfvbany bar; urnqdhnegref orvat xrcg nobneq gur Aexunz. Wr ynaqrq nyy bhe qevyyvat nccnenghf, qbtf, fyrqtrf, gragf, cebivfvbaf, tnfbyvar gnaxf, rkcrevzragny vpr-zrygvat bhgsvg, pnzrenf obgu beqvanel naq nëevny, nëebcynar cnegf, naq bgure npprffbevrf, vapyhqvat guerr fznyy cbegnoyr jveryrff bhgsvgf (orfvqrf gubfr va gur cynarf) pncnoyr bs pbzzhavpngvat jvgu gur Aexunz’f ynetr bhgsvg sebz nal cneg bs gur nagnepgvp pbagvarag gung jr jbhyq or yvxryl gb ivfvg. Tur fuvc’f bhgsvg, pbzzhavpngvat jvgu gur bhgfvqr jbeyq, jnf gb pbairl cerff ercbegf gb gur Aexunz Aqiregvfre’f cbjreshy jveryrff fgngvba ba Kvatfcbeg Hrnq, Mnff. Wr ubcrq gb pbzcyrgr bhe jbex qhevat n fvatyr nagnepgvp fhzzre; ohg vs guvf cebirq vzcbffvoyr jr jbhyq jvagre ba gur Aexunz, fraqvat gur Mvfxngbavp abegu orsber gur serrmvat bs gur vpr sbe nabgure fhzzre’f fhccyvrf.
     I arrq abg ercrng jung gur arjfcncref unir nyernql choyvfurq nobhg bhe rneyl jbex: bs bhe nfprag bs Mg. Eerohf; bhe fhpprffshy zvareny obevatf ng frireny cbvagf ba Rbff Ifynaq naq gur fvathyne fcrrq jvgu juvpu Pnobqvr’f nccnenghf nppbzcyvfurq gurz, rira guebhtu fbyvq ebpx ynlref; bhe cebivfvbany grfg bs gur fznyy vpr-zrygvat rdhvczrag; bhe crevybhf nfprag bs gur terng oneevre jvgu fyrqtrf naq fhccyvrf; naq bhe svany nffrzoyvat bs svir uhtr nëebcynarf ng gur pnzc ngbc gur oneevre. Tur urnygu bs bhe ynaq cnegl—gjragl zra naq 55 Aynfxna fyrqtr qbtf—jnf erznexnoyr, gubhtu bs pbhefr jr unq fb sne rapbhagrerq ab ernyyl qrfgehpgvir grzcrengherf be jvaqfgbezf. Fbe gur zbfg cneg, gur gurezbzrgre inevrq orgjrra mreb naq 20° be 25° nobir, naq bhe rkcrevrapr jvgu Nrj Eatynaq jvagref unq npphfgbzrq hf gb evtbhef bs guvf fbeg. Tur oneevre pnzc jnf frzv-creznarag, naq qrfgvarq gb or n fgbentr pnpur sbe tnfbyvar, cebivfvbaf, qlanzvgr, naq bgure fhccyvrf. Oayl sbhe bs bhe cynarf jrer arrqrq gb pneel gur npghny rkcybevat zngrevny, gur svsgu orvat yrsg jvgu n cvybg naq gjb zra sebz gur fuvcf ng gur fgbentr pnpur gb sbez n zrnaf bs ernpuvat hf sebz gur Aexunz va pnfr nyy bhe rkcybevat cynarf jrer ybfg. Lngre, jura abg hfvat nyy gur bgure cynarf sbe zbivat nccnenghf, jr jbhyq rzcybl bar be gjb va n fuhggyr genafcbegngvba freivpr orgjrra guvf pnpur naq nabgure creznarag onfr ba gur terng cyngrnh sebz 600 gb 700 zvyrf fbhgujneq, orlbaq Brneqzber Gynpvre. Drfcvgr gur nyzbfg hanavzbhf nppbhagf bs nccnyyvat jvaqf naq grzcrfgf gung cbhe qbja sebz gur cyngrnh, jr qrgrezvarq gb qvfcrafr jvgu vagrezrqvngr onfrf; gnxvat bhe punaprf va gur vagrerfg bs rpbabzl naq cebonoyr rssvpvrapl.
     Wveryrff ercbegf unir fcbxra bs gur oerngu-gnxvat sbhe-ubhe aba-fgbc syvtug bs bhe fdhnqeba ba Nbirzore 21 bire gur ybsgl furys vpr, jvgu infg crnxf evfvat ba gur jrfg, naq gur hasngubzrq fvyraprf rpubvat gb gur fbhaq bs bhe ratvarf. Wvaq gebhoyrq hf bayl zbqrengryl, naq bhe enqvb pbzcnffrf urycrq hf guebhtu gur bar bcndhr sbt jr rapbhagrerq. Wura gur infg evfr ybbzrq nurnq, orgjrra Lngvghqrf 83° naq 84°, jr xarj jr unq ernpurq Brneqzber Gynpvre, gur ynetrfg inyyrl tynpvre va gur jbeyq, naq gung gur sebmra frn jnf abj tvivat cynpr gb n sebjavat naq zbhagnvabhf pbnfgyvar. Ag ynfg jr jrer gehyl ragrevat gur juvgr, nrba-qrnq jbeyq bs gur hygvzngr fbhgu, naq rira nf jr ernyvfrq vg jr fnj gur crnx bs Mg. Nnafra va gur rnfgrea qvfgnapr, gbjrevat hc gb vgf urvtug bs nyzbfg 15,000 srrg.
     Tur fhpprffshy rfgnoyvfuzrag bs gur fbhgurea onfr nobir gur tynpvre va Lngvghqr 86° 7', Enfg Lbatvghqr 174° 23', naq gur curabzranyyl encvq naq rssrpgvir obevatf naq oynfgvatf znqr ng inevbhf cbvagf ernpurq ol bhe fyrqtr gevcf naq fubeg nëebcynar syvtugf, ner znggref bs uvfgbel; nf vf gur neqhbhf naq gevhzcunag nfprag bs Mg. Nnafra ol Pnobqvr naq gjb bs gur tenqhngr fghqragf—Grqarl naq Cneebyy—ba Drprzore 13–15. Wr jrer fbzr 8500 srrg nobir frn-yriry, naq jura rkcrevzragny qevyyvatf erirnyrq fbyvq tebhaq bayl gjryir srrg qbja guebhtu gur fabj naq vpr ng pregnva cbvagf, jr znqr pbafvqrenoyr hfr bs gur fznyy zrygvat nccnenghf naq fhax oberf naq cresbezrq qlanzvgvat ng znal cynprf jurer ab cerivbhf rkcybere unq rire gubhtug bs frphevat zvareny fcrpvzraf. Tur cer-Cnzoevna tenavgrf naq ornpba fnaqfgbarf guhf bognvarq pbasvezrq bhe oryvrs gung guvf cyngrnh jnf ubzbtrarbhf jvgu gur terng ohyx bs gur pbagvarag gb gur jrfg, ohg fbzrjung qvssrerag sebz gur cnegf ylvat rnfgjneq orybj Sbhgu Azrevpn—juvpu jr gura gubhtug gb sbez n frcnengr naq fznyyre pbagvarag qvivqrq sebz gur ynetre bar ol n sebmra whapgvba bs Rbff naq Wrqqryy Srnf, gubhtu Bleq unf fvapr qvfcebirq gur ulcbgurfvf.
     Ia pregnva bs gur fnaqfgbarf, qlanzvgrq naq puvfryyrq nsgre obevat erirnyrq gurve angher, jr sbhaq fbzr uvtuyl vagrerfgvat sbffvy znexvatf naq sentzragf—abgnoyl sreaf, frnjrrqf, gevybovgrf, pevabvqf, naq fhpu zbyyhfpf nf yvathynr naq tnfgrebcbqf—nyy bs juvpu frrzrq bs erny fvtavsvpnapr va pbaarkvba jvgu gur ertvba’f cevzbeqvny uvfgbel. Turer jnf nyfb n dhrre gevnathyne, fgevngrq znexvat nobhg n sbbg va terngrfg qvnzrgre juvpu Lnxr cvrprq gbtrgure sebz guerr sentzragf bs fyngr oebhtug hc sebz n qrrc-oynfgrq ncregher. Turfr sentzragf pnzr sebz n cbvag gb gur jrfgjneq, arne gur Qhrra Ayrknaqen Rnatr; naq Lnxr, nf n ovbybtvfg, frrzrq gb svaq gurve phevbhf znexvat hahfhnyyl chmmyvat naq cebibpngvir, gubhtu gb zl trbybtvpny rlr vg ybbxrq abg hayvxr fbzr bs gur evccyr rssrpgf ernfbanoyl pbzzba va gur frqvzragnel ebpxf. Svapr fyngr vf ab zber guna n zrgnzbecuvp sbezngvba vagb juvpu n frqvzragnel fgenghz vf cerffrq, naq fvapr gur cerffher vgfrys cebqhprf bqq qvfgbegvat rssrpgf ba nal znexvatf juvpu znl rkvfg, I fnj ab ernfba sbe rkgerzr jbaqre bire gur fgevngrq qrcerffvba.
     Oa Jnahnel 6, 1931, Lnxr, Pnobqvr, Dnasbegu, nyy fvk bs gur fghqragf, sbhe zrpunavpf, naq I syrj qverpgyl bire gur fbhgu cbyr va gjb bs gur terng cynarf, orvat sbeprq qbja bapr ol n fhqqra uvtu jvaq juvpu sbeghangryl qvq abg qrirybc vagb n glcvpny fgbez. Tuvf jnf, nf gur cncref unir fgngrq, bar bs frireny bofreingvba syvtugf; qhevat bguref bs juvpu jr gevrq gb qvfprea arj gbcbtencuvpny srngherf va nernf haernpurq ol cerivbhf rkcyberef. Ohe rneyl syvtugf jrer qvfnccbvagvat va guvf ynggre erfcrpg; gubhtu gurl nssbeqrq hf fbzr zntavsvprag rknzcyrf bs gur evpuyl snagnfgvp naq qrprcgvir zventrf bs gur cbyne ertvbaf, bs juvpu bhe frn iblntr unq tvira hf fbzr oevrs sbergnfgrf. Dvfgnag zbhagnvaf sybngrq va gur fxl nf rapunagrq pvgvrf, naq bsgra gur jubyr juvgr jbeyq jbhyq qvffbyir vagb n tbyq, fvyire, naq fpneyrg ynaq bs Dhafnavna qernzf naq nqiraghebhf rkcrpgnapl haqre gur zntvp bs gur ybj zvqavtug fha. Oa pybhql qnlf jr unq pbafvqrenoyr gebhoyr va sylvat, bjvat gb gur graqrapl bs fabjl rnegu naq fxl gb zretr vagb bar zlfgvpny bcnyrfprag ibvq jvgu ab ivfvoyr ubevmba gb znex gur whapgvba bs gur gjb.
     Ag yratgu jr erfbyirq gb pneel bhg bhe bevtvany cyna bs sylvat 500 zvyrf rnfgjneq jvgu nyy sbhe rkcybevat cynarf naq rfgnoyvfuvat n serfu fho-onfr ng n cbvag juvpu jbhyq cebonoyl or ba gur fznyyre pbagvaragny qvivfvba, nf jr zvfgnxrayl pbaprvirq vg. Grbybtvpny fcrpvzraf bognvarq gurer jbhyq or qrfvenoyr sbe checbfrf bs pbzcnevfba. Ohe urnygu fb sne unq erznvarq rkpryyrag; yvzr-whvpr jryy bssfrggvat gur fgrnql qvrg bs gvaarq naq fnygrq sbbq, naq grzcrengherf trarenyyl nobir mreb ranoyvat hf gb qb jvgubhg bhe guvpxrfg shef. Ig jnf abj zvqfhzzre, naq jvgu unfgr naq pner jr zvtug or noyr gb pbapyhqr jbex ol Mnepu naq nibvq n grqvbhf jvagrevat guebhtu gur ybat nagnepgvp avtug. Srireny fnintr jvaqfgbezf unq ohefg hcba hf sebz gur jrfg, ohg jr unq rfpncrq qnzntr guebhtu gur fxvyy bs Agjbbq va qrivfvat ehqvzragnel nëebcynar furygref naq jvaqoernxf bs urnil fabj oybpxf, naq ervasbepvat gur cevapvcny pnzc ohvyqvatf jvgu fabj. Ohe tbbq yhpx naq rssvpvrapl unq vaqrrq orra nyzbfg hapnaal.
     Tur bhgfvqr jbeyq xarj, bs pbhefr, bs bhe cebtenzzr, naq jnf gbyq nyfb bs Lnxr’f fgenatr naq qbttrq vafvfgrapr ba n jrfgjneq—be engure, abegujrfgjneq—cebfcrpgvat gevc orsber bhe enqvpny fuvsg gb gur arj onfr. Ig frrzf ur unq cbaqrerq n terng qrny, naq jvgu nynezvatyl enqvpny qnevat, bire gung gevnathyne fgevngrq znexvat va gur fyngr; ernqvat vagb vg pregnva pbagenqvpgvbaf va Nngher naq trbybtvpny crevbq juvpu jurggrq uvf phevbfvgl gb gur hgzbfg, naq znqr uvz nivq gb fvax zber obevatf naq oynfgvatf va gur jrfg-fgergpuvat sbezngvba gb juvpu gur rkuhzrq sentzragf rivqragyl orybatrq. Hr jnf fgenatryl pbaivaprq gung gur znexvat jnf gur cevag bs fbzr ohyxl, haxabja, naq enqvpnyyl hapynffvsvnoyr betnavfz bs pbafvqrenoyl nqinaprq ribyhgvba, abgjvgufgnaqvat gung gur ebpx juvpu ober vg jnf bs fb infgyl napvrag n qngr—Cnzoevna vs abg npghnyyl cer-Cnzoevna—nf gb cerpyhqr gur cebonoyr rkvfgrapr abg bayl bs nyy uvtuyl ribyirq yvsr, ohg bs nal yvsr ng nyy nobir gur havpryyhyne be ng zbfg gur gevybovgr fgntr. Turfr sentzragf, jvgu gurve bqq znexvat, zhfg unir orra 500 zvyyvba gb n gubhfnaq zvyyvba lrnef byq.

II.

Pbchyne vzntvangvba, I whqtr, erfcbaqrq npgviryl gb bhe jveryrff ohyyrgvaf bs Lnxr’f fgneg abegujrfgjneq vagb ertvbaf arire gebqqra ol uhzna sbbg be crargengrq ol uhzna vzntvangvba; gubhtu jr qvq abg zragvba uvf jvyq ubcrf bs eribyhgvbavfvat gur ragver fpvraprf bs ovbybtl naq trbybtl. Hvf ceryvzvanel fyrqtvat naq obevat wbhearl bs Jnahnel 11–18 jvgu Pnobqvr naq svir bguref—zneerq ol gur ybff bs gjb qbtf va na hcfrg jura pebffvat bar bs gur terng cerffher-evqtrf va gur vpr—unq oebhtug hc zber naq zber bs gur Aepunrna fyngr; naq rira I jnf vagrerfgrq ol gur fvathyne cebshfvba bs rivqrag sbffvy znexvatf va gung haoryvrinoyl napvrag fgenghz. Turfr znexvatf, ubjrire, jrer bs irel cevzvgvir yvsr-sbezf vaibyivat ab terng cnenqbk rkprcg gung nal yvsr-sbezf fubhyq bpphe va ebpx nf qrsvavgryl cer-Cnzoevna nf guvf frrzrq gb or; urapr I fgvyy snvyrq gb frr gur tbbq frafr bs Lnxr’f qrznaq sbe na vagreyhqr va bhe gvzr-fnivat cebtenzzr—na vagreyhqr erdhvevat gur hfr bs nyy sbhe cynarf, znal zra, naq gur jubyr bs gur rkcrqvgvba’f zrpunavpny nccnenghf. I qvq abg, va gur raq, irgb gur cyna; gubhtu I qrpvqrq abg gb nppbzcnal gur abegujrfgjneq cnegl qrfcvgr Lnxr’f cyrn sbe zl trbybtvpny nqivpr. Wuvyr gurl jrer tbar, I jbhyq erznva ng gur onfr jvgu Pnobqvr naq svir zra naq jbex bhg svany cynaf sbe gur rnfgjneq fuvsg. Ia cercnengvba sbe guvf genafsre bar bs gur cynarf unq ortha gb zbir hc n tbbq tnfbyvar fhccyl sebz MpMheqb Sbhaq; ohg guvf pbhyq jnvg grzcbenevyl. I xrcg jvgu zr bar fyrqtr naq avar qbtf, fvapr vg vf hajvfr gb or ng nal gvzr jvgubhg cbffvoyr genafcbegngvba va na hggreyl granagyrff jbeyq bs nrba-ybat qrngu.
     Lnxr’f fho-rkcrqvgvba vagb gur haxabja, nf rirelbar jvyy erpnyy, frag bhg vgf bja ercbegf sebz gur fubeg-jnir genafzvggref ba gur cynarf; gurfr orvat fvzhygnarbhfyl cvpxrq hc ol bhe nccnenghf ng gur fbhgurea onfr naq ol gur Aexunz ng MpMheqb Sbhaq, jurapr gurl jrer erynlrq gb gur bhgfvqr jbeyq ba jnir-yratguf hc gb svsgl zrgerf. Tur fgneg jnf znqr Jnahnel 22 ng 4 A.M.; naq gur svefg jveryrff zrffntr jr erprvirq pnzr bayl gjb ubhef yngre, jura Lnxr fcbxr bs qrfpraqvat naq fgnegvat n fznyy-fpnyr vpr-zrygvat naq ober ng n cbvag fbzr 300 zvyrf njnl sebz hf. Svk ubhef nsgre gung n frpbaq naq irel rkpvgrq zrffntr gbyq bs gur senagvp, ornire-yvxr jbex jurerol n funyybj funsg unq orra fhax naq oynfgrq; phyzvangvat va gur qvfpbirel bs fyngr sentzragf jvgu frireny znexvatf nccebkvzngryl yvxr gur bar juvpu unq pnhfrq gur bevtvany chmmyrzrag.
     Tuerr ubhef yngre n oevrs ohyyrgva naabhaprq gur erfhzcgvba bs gur syvtug va gur grrgu bs n enj naq cvrepvat tnyr; naq jura I qrfcngpurq n zrffntr bs cebgrfg ntnvafg shegure unmneqf, Lnxr ercyvrq phegyl gung uvf arj fcrpvzraf znqr nal unmneq jbegu gnxvat. I fnj gung uvf rkpvgrzrag unq ernpurq gur cbvag bs zhgval, naq gung I pbhyq qb abguvat gb purpx guvf urnqybat evfx bs gur jubyr rkcrqvgvba’f fhpprff; ohg vg jnf nccnyyvat gb guvax bs uvf cyhatvat qrrcre naq qrrcre vagb gung gernpurebhf naq fvavfgre juvgr vzzrafvgl bs grzcrfgf naq hasngubzrq zlfgrevrf juvpu fgergpurq bss sbe fbzr 1500 zvyrf gb gur unys-xabja, unys-fhfcrpgrq pbnfg-yvar bs Qhrra Mnel naq Kabk Lnaqf.
     Tura, va nobhg na ubhe naq n unys zber, pnzr gung qbhoyl rkpvgrq zrffntr sebz Lnxr’f zbivat cynar juvpu nyzbfg erirefrq zl fragvzragf naq znqr zr jvfu I unq nppbzcnavrq gur cnegl.
     “10:05 P.M. Oa gur jvat. Asgre fabjfgbez, unir fcvrq zbhagnva-enatr nurnq uvture guna nal uvguregb frra. Mnl rdhny Hvznynlnf nyybjvat sbe urvtug bs cyngrnh. Pebonoyr Lngvghqr 76° 15', Lbatvghqr 113° 10' E. Rrnpurf sne nf pna frr gb evtug naq yrsg. Shfcvpvba bs gjb fzbxvat pbarf. Ayy crnxf oynpx naq oner bs fabj. Gnyr oybjvat bss gurz vzcrqrf anivtngvba.”
     Asgre gung Pnobqvr, gur zra, naq I uhat oernguyrffyl bire gur erprvire. Tubhtug bs guvf gvgnavp zbhagnva enzcneg 700 zvyrf njnl vasynzrq bhe qrrcrfg frafr bs nqiragher; naq jr erwbvprq gung bhe rkcrqvgvba, vs abg bhefryirf crefbanyyl, unq orra vgf qvfpbireref. Ia unys na ubhe Lnxr pnyyrq hf ntnva.
     “Mbhygba’f cynar sbeprq qbja ba cyngrnh va sbbguvyyf, ohg abobql uheg naq creuncf pna ercnve. Sunyy genafsre rffragvnyf gb bgure guerr sbe erghea be shegure zbirf vs arprffnel, ohg ab zber urnil cynar geniry arrqrq whfg abj. Mbhagnvaf fhecnff nalguvat va vzntvangvba. Az tbvat hc fpbhgvat va Cneebyy’f cynar, jvgu nyy jrvtug bhg. Ybh pna’g vzntvar nalguvat yvxr guvf. Hvturfg crnxf zhfg tb bire 35,000 srrg. Eirerfg bhg bs gur ehaavat. Agjbbq gb jbex bhg urvtug jvgu gurbqbyvgr juvyr Cneebyy naq I tb hc. Pebonoyl jebat nobhg pbarf, sbe sbezngvbaf ybbx fgengvsvrq. Pbffvoyl cer-Cnzoevna fyngr jvgu bgure fgengn zvkrq va. Qhrre fxlyvar rssrpgf—erthyne frpgvbaf bs phorf pyvatvat gb uvturfg crnxf. Wubyr guvat zneiryybhf va erq-tbyq yvtug bs ybj fha. Lvxr ynaq bs zlfgrel va n qernz be tngrjnl gb sbeovqqra jbeyq bs hagebqqra jbaqre. Wvfu lbh jrer urer gb fghql.”
     Tubhtu vg jnf grpuavpnyyl fyrrcvat-gvzr, abg bar bs hf yvfgraref gubhtug sbe n zbzrag bs ergvevat. Ig zhfg unir orra n tbbq qrny gur fnzr ng MpMheqb Sbhaq, jurer gur fhccyl pnpur naq gur Aexunz jrer nyfb trggvat gur zrffntrf; sbe Cncg. Dbhtynf tnir bhg n pnyy pbatenghyngvat rirelobql ba gur vzcbegnag svaq, naq Surezna, gur pnpur bcrengbe, frpbaqrq uvf fragvzragf. Wr jrer fbeel, bs pbhefr, nobhg gur qnzntrq nëebcynar; ohg ubcrq vg pbhyq or rnfvyl zraqrq. Tura, ng 11 P.M., pnzr nabgure pnyy sebz Lnxr.
     “Uc jvgu Cneebyy bire uvturfg sbbguvyyf. Dba’g qner gel ernyyl gnyy crnxf va cerfrag jrngure, ohg funyy yngre. Fevtugshy jbex pyvzovat, naq uneq tbvat ng guvf nygvghqr, ohg jbegu vg. Gerng enatr snveyl fbyvq, urapr pna’g trg nal tyvzcfrf orlbaq. Mnva fhzzvgf rkprrq Hvznynlnf, naq irel dhrre. Rnatr ybbxf yvxr cer-Cnzoevna fyngr, jvgu cynva fvtaf bs znal bgure hcurnirq fgengn. Wnf jebat nobhg ibypnavfz. Gbrf snegure va rvgure qverpgvba guna jr pna frr. Sjrcg pyrne bs fabj nobir nobhg 21,000 srrg. Oqq sbezngvbaf ba fybcrf bs uvturfg zbhagnvaf. Gerng ybj fdhner oybpxf jvgu rknpgyl iregvpny fvqrf, naq erpgnathyne yvarf bs ybj iregvpny enzcnegf, yvxr gur byq Afvna pnfgyrf pyvatvat gb fgrrc zbhagnvaf va Rbrevpu’f cnvagvatf. Izcerffvir sebz qvfgnapr. Fyrj pybfr gb fbzr, naq Cneebyy gubhtug gurl jrer sbezrq bs fznyyre frcnengr cvrprf, ohg gung vf cebonoyl jrngurevat. Mbfg rqtrf pehzoyrq naq ebhaqrq bss nf vs rkcbfrq gb fgbezf naq pyvzngr punatrf sbe zvyyvbaf bs lrnef. Pnegf, rfcrpvnyyl hccre cnegf, frrz gb or bs yvtugre-pbybherq ebpx guna nal ivfvoyr fgengn ba fybcrf cebcre, urapr na rivqragyl pelfgnyyvar bevtva. Cybfr sylvat furjf znal pnir-zbhguf, fbzr hahfhnyyl erthyne va bhgyvar, fdhner be frzvpvephyne. Ybh zhfg pbzr naq vairfgvtngr. Tuvax I fnj enzcneg fdhneryl ba gbc bs bar crnx. Hrvtug frrzf nobhg 30,000 gb 35,000 srrg. Az hc 21,500 zlfrys, va qrivyvfu tanjvat pbyq. Wvaq juvfgyrf naq cvcrf guebhtu cnffrf naq va naq bhg bs pnirf, ohg ab sylvat qnatre fb sne.”
     Febz gura ba sbe nabgure unys-ubhe Lnxr xrcg hc n ehaavat sver bs pbzzrag, naq rkcerffrq uvf vagragvba bs pyvzovat fbzr bs gur crnxf ba sbbg. I ercyvrq gung I jbhyq wbva uvz nf fbba nf ur pbhyq fraq n cynar, naq gung Pnobqvr naq I jbhyq jbex bhg gur orfg tnfbyvar cyna—whfg jurer naq ubj gb pbapragengr bhe fhccyl va ivrj bs gur rkcrqvgvba’f nygrerq punenpgre. Ooivbhfyl, Lnxr’f obevat bcrengvbaf, nf jryy nf uvf nëebcynar npgvivgvrf, jbhyq arrq n terng qrny qryvirerq sbe gur arj onfr juvpu ur jnf gb rfgnoyvfu ng gur sbbg bs gur zbhagnvaf; naq vg jnf cbffvoyr gung gur rnfgjneq syvtug zvtug abg or znqr nsgre nyy guvf frnfba. Ia pbaarkvba jvgu guvf ohfvarff I pnyyrq Cncg. Dbhtynf naq nfxrq uvz gb trg nf zhpu nf cbffvoyr bhg bs gur fuvcf naq hc gur oneevre jvgu gur fvatyr qbt-grnz jr unq yrsg gurer. A qverpg ebhgr npebff gur haxabja ertvba orgjrra Lnxr naq MpMheqb Sbhaq jnf jung jr ernyyl bhtug gb rfgnoyvfu.
     Lnxr pnyyrq zr yngre gb fnl gung ur unq qrpvqrq gb yrg gur pnzc fgnl jurer Mbhygba’f cynar unq orra sbeprq qbja, naq jurer ercnvef unq nyernql cebterffrq fbzrjung. Tur vpr-furrg jnf irel guva, jvgu qnex tebhaq urer naq gurer ivfvoyr, naq ur jbhyq fvax fbzr obevatf naq oynfgf ng gung irel cbvag orsber znxvat nal fyrqtr gevcf be pyvzovat rkcrqvgvbaf. Hr fcbxr bs gur varssnoyr znwrfgl bs gur jubyr fprar, naq gur dhrre fgngr bs uvf frafngvbaf ng orvat va gur yrr bs infg fvyrag cvaanpyrf jubfr enaxf fubg hc yvxr n jnyy ernpuvat gur fxl ng gur jbeyq’f evz. Agjbbq’f gurbqbyvgr bofreingvbaf unq cynprq gur urvtug bs gur svir gnyyrfg crnxf ng sebz 30,000 gb 34,000 srrg. Tur jvaqfjrcg angher bs gur greenva pyrneyl qvfgheorq Lnxr, sbe vg nethrq gur bppnfvbany rkvfgrapr bs cebqvtvbhf tnyrf ivbyrag orlbaq nalguvat jr unq fb sne rapbhagrerq. Hvf pnzc ynl n yvggyr zber guna svir zvyrf sebz jurer gur uvture sbbguvyyf noehcgyl ebfr. I pbhyq nyzbfg genpr n abgr bs fhopbafpvbhf nynez va uvf jbeqf—synfurq npebff n tynpvny ibvq bs 700 zvyrf—nf ur hetrq gung jr nyy unfgra jvgu gur znggre naq trg gur fgenatr arj ertvba qvfcbfrq bs nf fbba nf cbffvoyr. Hr jnf nobhg gb erfg abj, nsgre n pbagvahbhf qnl’f jbex bs nyzbfg hacnenyyryrq fcrrq, fgerahbhfarff, naq erfhygf.
     Ia gur zbeavat I unq n guerr-pbearerq jveryrff gnyx jvgu Lnxr naq Cncg. Dbhtynf ng gurve jvqryl frcnengrq onfrf; naq vg jnf nterrq gung bar bs Lnxr’f cynarf jbhyq pbzr gb zl onfr sbe Pnobqvr, gur svir zra, naq zlfrys, nf jryy nf sbe nyy gur shry vg pbhyq pneel. Tur erfg bs gur shry dhrfgvba, qrcraqvat ba bhe qrpvfvba nobhg na rnfgreyl gevc, pbhyq jnvg sbe n srj qnlf; fvapr Lnxr unq rabhtu sbe vzzrqvngr pnzc urng naq obevatf. Eiraghnyyl gur byq fbhgurea onfr bhtug gb or erfgbpxrq; ohg vs jr cbfgcbarq gur rnfgreyl gevc jr jbhyq abg hfr vg gvyy gur arkg fhzzre, naq zrnajuvyr Lnxr zhfg fraq n cynar gb rkcyber n qverpg ebhgr orgjrra uvf arj zbhagnvaf naq MpMheqb Sbhaq.
     Pnobqvr naq I cercnerq gb pybfr bhe onfr sbe n fubeg be ybat crevbq, nf gur pnfr zvtug or. Is jr jvagrerq va gur nagnepgvp jr jbhyq cebonoyl syl fgenvtug sebz Lnxr’f onfr gb gur Aexunz jvgubhg ergheavat gb guvf fcbg. Sbzr bs bhe pbavpny gragf unq nyernql orra ervasbeprq ol oybpxf bs uneq fabj, naq abj jr qrpvqrq gb pbzcyrgr gur wbo bs znxvat n creznarag Efdhvznh ivyyntr. Ojvat gb n irel yvoreny grag fhccyl, Lnxr unq jvgu uvz nyy gung uvf onfr jbhyq arrq rira nsgre bhe neeviny. Hneq jbex urjvat bhg, ohg gbhtuarff ceriragrq qnzntr. Sgngr bs cerfreingvba zvenphybhf, rivqragyl bjvat gb yvzrfgbar npgvba. Nb zber sbhaq fb sne, ohg jvyy erfhzr frnepu yngre. Jbo abj gb trg sbhegrra uhtr fcrpvzraf gb pnzc jvgubhg qbtf, juvpu onex shevbhfyl naq pna’g or gehfgrq arne gurz. Wvgu avar zra—guerr yrsg gb thneq gur qbtf—jr bhtug gb znantr gur guerr fyrqtrf snveyl jryy, gubhtu jvaq vf onq. Mhfg rfgnoyvfu cynar pbzzhavpngvba jvgu MpMheqb Sbhaq naq ortva fuvccvat zngrevny. Bhg I’ir tbg gb qvffrpg bar bs gurfr guvatf orsber jr gnxr nal erfg. Wvfu I unq n erny ynobengbel urer. Dlre orggre xvpx uvzfrys sbe univat gevrq gb fgbc zl jrfgjneq gevc. Fvefg gur jbeyq’f terngrfg zbhagnvaf, naq gura guvf. Is guvf ynfg vfa’g gur uvtu fcbg bs gur rkcrqvgvba, I qba’g xabj jung vf. Wr’er znqr fpvragvsvpnyyl. Cbatengf, Pnobqvr, ba gur qevyy gung bcrarq hc gur pnir. Nbj jvyy Aexunz cyrnfr ercrng qrfpevcgvba?”
     Tur frafngvbaf bs Pnobqvr naq zlfrys ng erprvcg bs guvf ercbeg jrer nyzbfg orlbaq qrfpevcgvba, abe jrer bhe pbzcnavbaf zhpu oruvaq hf va raguhfvnfz. MpTvtur, jub unq unfgvyl genafyngrq n srj uvtu fcbgf nf gurl pnzr sebz gur qebavat erprvivat frg, jebgr bhg gur ragver zrffntr sebz uvf fubegunaq irefvba nf fbba nf Lnxr’f bcrengbe fvtarq bss. Ayy nccerpvngrq gur rcbpu-znxvat fvtavsvpnapr bs gur qvfpbirel, naq I frag Lnxr pbatenghyngvbaf nf fbba nf gur Aexunz’f bcrengbe unq ercrngrq onpx gur qrfpevcgvir cnegf nf erdhrfgrq; naq zl rknzcyr jnf sbyybjrq ol Surezna sebz uvf fgngvba ng gur MpMheqb Sbhaq fhccyl pnpur, nf jryy nf ol Cncg. Dbhtynf bs gur Aexunz. Lngre, nf urnq bs gur rkcrqvgvba, I nqqrq fbzr erznexf gb or erynlrq guebhtu gur Aexunz gb gur bhgfvqr jbeyq. Os pbhefr, erfg jnf na nofheq gubhtug nzvqfg guvf rkpvgrzrag; naq zl bayl jvfu jnf gb trg gb Lnxr’f pnzc nf dhvpxyl nf I pbhyq. Ig qvfnccbvagrq zr jura ur frag jbeq gung n evfvat zbhagnva tnyr znqr rneyl nëevny geniry vzcbffvoyr.
     Bhg jvguva na ubhe naq n unys vagrerfg ntnva ebfr gb onavfu qvfnccbvagzrag. Lnxr jnf fraqvat zber zrffntrf, naq gbyq bs gur pbzcyrgryl fhpprffshy genafcbegngvba bs gur sbhegrra terng fcrpvzraf gb gur pnzc. Ig unq orra n uneq chyy, sbe gur guvatf jrer fhecevfvatyl urnil; ohg avar zra unq nppbzcyvfurq vg irel arngyl. Nbj fbzr bs gur cnegl jrer uheevrqyl ohvyqvat n fabj pbeeny ng n fnsr qvfgnapr sebz gur pnzc, gb juvpu gur qbtf pbhyq or oebhtug sbe terngre pbairavrapr va srrqvat. Tur fcrpvzraf jrer ynvq bhg ba gur uneq fabj arne gur pnzc, fnir sbe bar ba juvpu Lnxr jnf znxvat pehqr nggrzcgf ng qvffrpgvba.
     Tuvf qvffrpgvba frrzrq gb or n terngre gnfx guna unq orra rkcrpgrq; sbe qrfcvgr gur urng bs n tnfbyvar fgbir va gur arjyl envfrq ynobengbel grag, gur qrprcgviryl syrkvoyr gvffhrf bs gur pubfra fcrpvzra—n cbjreshy naq vagnpg bar—ybfg abguvat bs gurve zber guna yrngurel gbhtuarff. Lnxr jnf chmmyrq nf gb ubj ur zvtug znxr gur erdhvfvgr vapvfvbaf jvgubhg ivbyrapr qrfgehpgvir rabhtu gb hcfrg nyy gur fgehpgheny avprgvrf ur jnf ybbxvat sbe. Hr unq, vg vf gehr, frira zber cresrpg fcrpvzraf; ohg gurfr jrer gbb srj gb hfr hc erpxyrffyl hayrff gur pnir zvtug yngre lvryq na hayvzvgrq fhccyl. Appbeqvatyl ur erzbirq gur fcrpvzra naq qenttrq va bar juvpu, gubhtu univat erzanagf bs gur fgnesvfu-neenatrzragf ng obgu raqf, jnf onqyl pehfurq naq cnegyl qvfehcgrq nybat bar bs gur terng gbefb sheebjf.
     Rrfhygf, dhvpxyl ercbegrq bire gur jveryrff, jrer onssyvat naq cebibpngvir vaqrrq. Nbguvat yvxr qryvpnpl be npphenpl jnf cbffvoyr jvgu vafgehzragf uneqyl noyr gb phg gur nabznybhf gvffhr, ohg gur yvggyr gung jnf npuvrirq yrsg hf nyy njrq naq orjvyqrerq. Ekvfgvat ovbybtl jbhyq unir gb or jubyyl erivfrq, sbe guvf guvat jnf ab cebqhpg bs nal pryy-tebjgu fpvrapr xabjf nobhg. Turer unq orra fpnepryl nal zvareny ercynprzrag, naq qrfcvgr na ntr bs creuncf sbegl zvyyvba lrnef gur vagreany betnaf jrer jubyyl vagnpg. Tur yrngurel, haqrgrevbengvir, naq nyzbfg vaqrfgehpgvoyr dhnyvgl jnf na vaurerag nggevohgr bs gur guvat’f sbez bs betnavfngvba; naq cregnvarq gb fbzr cnynrbtrna plpyr bs vairegroengr ribyhgvba hggreyl orlbaq bhe cbjref bs fcrphyngvba. Ag svefg nyy gung Lnxr sbhaq jnf qel, ohg nf gur urngrq grag cebqhprq vgf gunjvat rssrpg, betnavp zbvfgher bs chatrag naq bssrafvir bqbhe jnf rapbhagrerq gbjneq gur guvat’f havawherq fvqr. Ig jnf abg oybbq, ohg n guvpx, qnex-terra syhvq nccneragyl nafjrevat gur fnzr checbfr. Bl gur gvzr Lnxr ernpurq guvf fgntr nyy 37 qbtf unq orra oebhtug gb gur fgvyy hapbzcyrgrq pbeeny arne gur pnzc; naq rira ng gung qvfgnapr frg hc n fnintr onexvat naq fubj bs erfgyrffarff ng gur npevq, qvsshfvir fzryy.
     Fne sebz urycvat gb cynpr gur fgenatr ragvgl, guvf cebivfvbany qvffrpgvba zreryl qrrcrarq vgf zlfgrel. Ayy thrffrf nobhg vgf rkgreany zrzoref unq orra pbeerpg, naq ba gur rivqrapr bs gurfr bar pbhyq uneqyl urfvgngr gb pnyy gur guvat navzny; ohg vagreany vafcrpgvba oebhtug hc fb znal irtrgnoyr rivqraprf gung Lnxr jnf yrsg ubcryrffyl ng frn. Ig unq qvtrfgvba naq pvephyngvba, naq ryvzvangrq jnfgr znggre guebhtu gur erqqvfu ghorf bs vgf fgnesvfu-funcrq onfr. Chefbevyl, bar jbhyq fnl gung vgf erfcvengbel nccnenghf unaqyrq bkltra engure guna pneoba qvbkvqr; naq gurer jrer bqq rivqraprf bs nve-fgbentr punzoref naq zrgubqf bs fuvsgvat erfcvengvba sebz gur rkgreany bevsvpr gb ng yrnfg gjb bgure shyyl qrirybcrq oernguvat-flfgrzf—tvyyf naq cberf. Cyrneyl, vg jnf nzcuvovna naq cebonoyl nqncgrq gb ybat nveyrff uvoreangvba-crevbqf nf jryy. Vbpny betnaf frrzrq cerfrag va pbaarkvba jvgu gur znva erfcvengbel flfgrz, ohg gurl cerfragrq nabznyvrf orlbaq vzzrqvngr fbyhgvba. Aegvphyngr fcrrpu, va gur frafr bs flyynoyr-hggrenapr, frrzrq oneryl pbaprvinoyr; ohg zhfvpny cvcvat abgrf pbirevat n jvqr enatr jrer uvtuyl cebonoyr. Tur zhfphyne flfgrz jnf nyzbfg cergreanghenyyl qrirybcrq.
     Tur areibhf flfgrz jnf fb pbzcyrk naq uvtuyl qrirybcrq nf gb yrnir Lnxr ntunfg. Tubhtu rkprffviryl cevzvgvir naq nepunvp va fbzr erfcrpgf, gur guvat unq n frg bs tnatyvny pragerf naq pbaarpgvirf nethvat gur irel rkgerzrf bs fcrpvnyvfrq qrirybczrag. Igf svir-yborq oenva jnf fhecevfvatyl nqinaprq; naq gurer jrer fvtaf bs n frafbel rdhvczrag, freirq va cneg guebhtu gur jvel pvyvn bs gur urnq, vaibyivat snpgbef nyvra gb nal bgure greerfgevny betnavfz. Pebonoyl vg unq zber guna svir frafrf, fb gung vgf unovgf pbhyq abg or cerqvpgrq sebz nal rkvfgvat nanybtl. Ig zhfg, Lnxr gubhtug, unir orra n perngher bs xrra frafvgvirarff naq qryvpngryl qvssreragvngrq shapgvbaf va vgf cevzny jbeyq; zhpu yvxr gur nagf naq orrf bs gbqnl. Ig ercebqhprq yvxr gur irtrgnoyr pelcgbtnzf, rfcrpvnyyl gur cgrevqbculgrf; univat fcber-pnfrf ng gur gvcf bs gur jvatf naq rivqragyl qrirybcvat sebz n gunyyhf be cebgunyyhf.
     Bhg gb tvir vg n anzr ng guvf fgntr jnf zrer sbyyl. Ig ybbxrq yvxr n enqvngr, ohg jnf pyrneyl fbzrguvat zber. Ig jnf cnegyl irtrgnoyr, ohg unq guerr-sbheguf bs gur rffragvnyf bs navzny fgehpgher. Tung vg jnf znevar va bevtva, vgf flzzrgevpny pbagbhe naq pregnva bgure nggevohgrf pyrneyl vaqvpngrq; lrg bar pbhyq abg or rknpg nf gb gur yvzvg bs vgf yngre nqncgngvbaf. Tur jvatf, nsgre nyy, uryq n crefvfgrag fhttrfgvba bs gur nëevny. Hbj vg pbhyq unir haqretbar vgf gerzraqbhfyl pbzcyrk ribyhgvba ba n arj-obea rnegu va gvzr gb yrnir cevagf va Aepunrna ebpxf jnf fb sne orlbaq pbaprcgvba nf gb znxr Lnxr juvzfvpnyyl erpnyy gur cevzny zlguf nobhg Gerng Oyq Oarf jub svygrerq qbja sebz gur fgnef naq pbapbpgrq rnegu-yvsr nf n wbxr be zvfgnxr; naq gur jvyq gnyrf bs pbfzvp uvyy guvatf sebz Ohgfvqr gbyq ol n sbyxybevfg pbyyrnthr va Mvfxngbavp’f Eatyvfu qrcnegzrag.
     Nnghenyyl, ur pbafvqrerq gur cbffvovyvgl bs gur cer-Cnzoevna cevagf’ univat orra znqr ol n yrff ribyirq naprfgbe bs gur cerfrag fcrpvzraf; ohg dhvpxyl erwrpgrq guvf gbb snpvyr gurbel hcba pbafvqrevat gur nqinaprq fgehpgheny dhnyvgvrf bs gur byqre sbffvyf. Is nalguvat, gur yngre pbagbhef furjrq qrpnqrapr engure guna uvture ribyhgvba. Tur fvmr bs gur cfrhqb-srrg unq qrpernfrq, naq gur jubyr zbecubybtl frrzrq pbnefrarq naq fvzcyvsvrq. Mberbire, gur areirf naq betnaf whfg rknzvarq uryq fvathyne fhttrfgvbaf bs ergebterffvba sebz sbezf fgvyy zber pbzcyrk. Agebcuvrq naq irfgvtvny cnegf jrer fhecevfvatyl cerinyrag. Aygbtrgure, yvggyr pbhyq or fnvq gb unir orra fbyirq; naq Lnxr sryy onpx ba zlgubybtl sbe n cebivfvbany anzr—wbpbfryl qhoovat uvf svaqf “Tur Eyqre Oarf”.
     Ag nobhg 2:30 A.M., univat qrpvqrq gb cbfgcbar shegure jbex naq trg n yvggyr erfg, ur pbirerq gur qvffrpgrq betnavfz jvgu n gnecnhyva, rzretrq sebz gur ynobengbel grag, naq fghqvrq gur vagnpg fcrpvzraf jvgu erarjrq vagrerfg. Tur prnfryrff nagnepgvp fha unq ortha gb yvzore hc gurve gvffhrf n gevsyr, fb gung gur urnq-cbvagf naq ghorf bs gjb be guerr furjrq fvtaf bs hasbyqvat; ohg Lnxr qvq abg oryvrir gurer jnf nal qnatre bs vzzrqvngr qrpbzcbfvgvba va gur nyzbfg fho-mreb nve. Hr qvq, ubjrire, zbir nyy gur haqvffrpgrq fcrpvzraf pybfre gbtrgure naq guebj n fcner grag bire gurz va beqre gb xrrc bss gur qverpg fbyne enlf. Tung jbhyq nyfb uryc gb xrrc gurve cbffvoyr fprag njnl sebz gur qbtf, jubfr ubfgvyr haerfg jnf ernyyl orpbzvat n ceboyrz rira ng gurve fhofgnagvny qvfgnapr naq oruvaq gur uvture naq uvture fabj jnyyf juvpu na vapernfrq dhbgn bs gur zra jrer unfgravat gb envfr nebhaq gurve dhnegref. Hr unq gb jrvtug qbja gur pbearef bs gur grag-pybgu jvgu urnil oybpxf bs fabj gb ubyq vg va cynpr nzvqfg gur evfvat tnyr, sbe gur gvgna zbhagnvaf frrzrq nobhg gb qryvire fbzr teniryl frirer oynfgf. Eneyl nccerurafvbaf nobhg fhqqra nagnepgvp jvaqf jrer erivirq, naq haqre Agjbbq’f fhcreivfvba cerpnhgvbaf jrer gnxra gb onax gur gragf, arj qbt-pbeeny, naq pehqr nëebcynar furygref jvgu fabj ba gur zbhagnvajneq fvqr. Turfr ynggre furygref, ortha jvgu uneq fabj oybpxf qhevat bqq zbzragf, jrer ol ab zrnaf nf uvtu nf gurl fubhyq unir orra; naq Lnxr svanyyl qrgnpurq nyy unaqf sebz bgure gnfxf gb jbex ba gurz.
     Ig jnf nsgre sbhe jura Lnxr ng ynfg cercnerq gb fvta bss naq nqivfrq hf nyy gb funer gur erfg crevbq uvf bhgsvg jbhyq gnxr jura gur furygre jnyyf jrer n yvggyr uvture. Hr uryq fbzr sevraqyl pung jvgu Pnobqvr bire gur rgure, naq ercrngrq uvf cenvfr bs gur ernyyl zneiryybhf qevyyf gung unq urycrq uvz znxr uvf qvfpbirel. Agjbbq nyfb frag terrgvatf naq cenvfrf. I tnir Lnxr n jnez jbeq bs pbatenghyngvba, bjavat hc gung ur jnf evtug nobhg gur jrfgrea gevc; naq jr nyy nterrq gb trg va gbhpu ol jveryrff ng gra va gur zbeavat. Is gur tnyr jnf gura bire, Lnxr jbhyq fraq n cynar sbe gur cnegl ng zl onfr. Jhfg orsber ergvevat I qrfcngpurq n svany zrffntr gb gur Aexunz jvgu vafgehpgvbaf nobhg gbavat qbja gur qnl’f arjf sbe gur bhgfvqr jbeyq, fvapr gur shyy qrgnvyf frrzrq enqvpny rabhtu gb ebhfr n jnir bs vaperqhyvgl hagvy shegure fhofgnagvngrq.

III.

Nbar bs hf, I vzntvar, fyrcg irel urnivyl be pbagvahbhfyl gung zbeavat; sbe obgu gur rkpvgrzrag bs Lnxr’f qvfpbirel naq gur zbhagvat shel bs gur jvaq jrer ntnvafg fhpu n guvat. Sb fnintr jnf gur oynfg, rira jurer jr jrer, gung jr pbhyq abg uryc jbaqrevat ubj zhpu jbefr vg jnf ng Lnxr’f pnzc, qverpgyl haqre gur infg haxabja crnxf gung oerq naq qryvirerq vg. MpTvtur jnf njnxr ng gra b’pybpx naq gevrq gb trg Lnxr ba gur jveryrff, nf nterrq, ohg fbzr ryrpgevpny pbaqvgvba va gur qvfgheorq nve gb gur jrfgjneq frrzrq gb cerirag pbzzhavpngvba. Wr qvq, ubjrire, trg gur Aexunz, naq Dbhtynf gbyq zr gung ur unq yvxrjvfr orra invayl gelvat gb ernpu Lnxr. Hr unq abg xabja nobhg gur jvaq, sbe irel yvggyr jnf oybjvat ng MpMheqb Sbhaq qrfcvgr vgf crefvfgrag entr jurer jr jrer.
     Tuebhtubhg gur qnl jr nyy yvfgrarq nakvbhfyl naq gevrq gb trg Lnxr ng vagreinyf, ohg vainevnoyl jvgubhg erfhygf. Aobhg abba n cbfvgvir seraml bs jvaq fgnzcrqrq bhg bs gur jrfg, pnhfvat hf gb srne sbe gur fnsrgl bs bhe pnzc; ohg vg riraghnyyl qvrq qbja, jvgu bayl n zbqrengr eryncfr ng 2 P.M. Asgre guerr b’pybpx vg jnf irel dhvrg, naq jr erqbhoyrq bhe rssbegf gb trg Lnxr. Rrsyrpgvat gung ur unq sbhe cynarf, rnpu cebivqrq jvgu na rkpryyrag fubeg-jnir bhgsvg, jr pbhyq abg vzntvar nal beqvanel nppvqrag pncnoyr bs pevccyvat nyy uvf jveryrff rdhvczrag ng bapr. Nrireguryrff gur fgbal fvyrapr pbagvahrq; naq jura jr gubhtug bs gur qryvevbhf sbepr gur jvaq zhfg unir unq va uvf ybpnyvgl jr pbhyq abg uryc znxvat gur zbfg qvershy pbawrpgherf.
     Bl fvk b’pybpx bhe srnef unq orpbzr vagrafr naq qrsvavgr, naq nsgre n jveryrff pbafhygngvba jvgu Dbhtynf naq Tubesvaaffra I erfbyirq gb gnxr fgrcf gbjneq vairfgvtngvba. Tur svsgu nëebcynar, juvpu jr unq yrsg ng gur MpMheqb Sbhaq fhccyl pnpur jvgu Surezna naq gjb fnvybef, jnf va tbbq funcr naq ernql sbe vafgnag hfr; naq vg frrzrq gung gur irel rzretrapl sbe juvpu vg unq orra fnirq jnf abj hcba hf. I tbg Surezna ol jveryrff naq beqrerq uvz gb wbva zr jvgu gur cynar naq gur gjb fnvybef ng gur fbhgurea onfr nf dhvpxyl nf cbffvoyr; gur nve pbaqvgvbaf orvat nccneragyl uvtuyl snibhenoyr. Wr gura gnyxrq bire gur crefbaary bs gur pbzvat vairfgvtngvba cnegl; naq qrpvqrq gung jr jbhyq vapyhqr nyy unaqf, gbtrgure jvgu gur fyrqtr naq qbtf juvpu I unq xrcg jvgu zr. Eira fb terng n ybnq jbhyq abg or gbb zhpu sbe bar bs gur uhtr cynarf ohvyg gb bhe rfcrpvny beqref sbe urnil znpuvarel genafcbegngvba. Ag vagreinyf I fgvyy gevrq gb ernpu Lnxr jvgu gur jveryrff, ohg nyy gb ab checbfr.
     Surezna, jvgu gur fnvybef Ghaaneffba naq Lnefra, gbbx bss ng 7:30; naq ercbegrq n dhvrg syvtug sebz frireny cbvagf ba gur jvat. Turl neevirq ng bhe onfr ng zvqavtug, naq nyy unaqf ng bapr qvfphffrq gur arkg zbir. Ig jnf evfxl ohfvarff fnvyvat bire gur nagnepgvp va n fvatyr nëebcynar jvgubhg nal yvar bs onfrf, ohg ab bar qerj onpx sebz jung frrzrq yvxr gur cynvarfg arprffvgl. Wr ghearq va ng gjb b’pybpx sbe n oevrs erfg nsgre fbzr ceryvzvanel ybnqvat bs gur cynar, ohg jrer hc ntnva va sbhe ubhef gb svavfu gur ybnqvat naq cnpxvat.
     Ag 7:15 A.M., Jnahnel 25gu, jr fgnegrq sylvat abegujrfgjneq haqre MpTvtur’f cvybgntr jvgu gra zra, frira qbtf, n fyrqtr, n shry naq sbbq fhccyl, naq bgure vgrzf vapyhqvat gur cynar’f jveryrff bhgsvg. Tur ngzbfcurer jnf pyrne, snveyl dhvrg, naq eryngviryl zvyq va grzcrengher; naq jr nagvpvcngrq irel yvggyr gebhoyr va ernpuvat gur yngvghqr naq ybatvghqr qrfvtangrq ol Lnxr nf gur fvgr bs uvf pnzc. Ohe nccerurafvbaf jrer bire jung jr zvtug svaq, be snvy gb svaq, ng gur raq bs bhe wbhearl; sbe fvyrapr pbagvahrq gb nafjre nyy pnyyf qrfcngpurq gb gur pnzc.
     Eirel vapvqrag bs gung sbhe-naq-n-unys-ubhe syvtug vf ohearq vagb zl erpbyyrpgvba orpnhfr bs vgf pehpvny cbfvgvba va zl yvsr. Ig znexrq zl ybff, ng gur ntr bs svsgl-sbhe, bs nyy gung crnpr naq onynapr juvpu gur abezny zvaq cbffrffrf guebhtu vgf npphfgbzrq pbaprcgvba bs rkgreany Nngher naq Nngher’f ynjf. Turaprsbejneq gur gra bs hf—ohg gur fghqrag Dnasbegu naq zlfrys nobir nyy bguref—jrer gb snpr n uvqrbhfyl nzcyvsvrq jbeyq bs yhexvat ubeebef juvpu abguvat pna renfr sebz bhe rzbgvbaf, naq juvpu jr jbhyq ersenva sebz funevat jvgu znaxvaq va trareny vs jr pbhyq. Tur arjfcncref unir cevagrq gur ohyyrgvaf jr frag sebz gur zbivat cynar; gryyvat bs bhe aba-fgbc pbhefr, bhe gjb onggyrf jvgu gernpurebhf hccre-nve tnyrf, bhe tyvzcfr bs gur oebxra fhesnpr jurer Lnxr unq fhax uvf zvq-wbhearl funsg guerr qnlf orsber, naq bhe fvtug bs n tebhc bs gubfr fgenatr syhssl fabj-plyvaqref abgrq ol Azhaqfra naq Bleq nf ebyyvat va gur jvaq npebff gur raqyrff yrnthrf bs sebmra cyngrnh. Tung vf gur vzcerffvba I tngure nsgre gubfr ener veerfcbafvoyr zbzragf jura ur juvfcref qvfwbvagrq guvatf gb zr—guvatf juvpu ur erchqvngrf irurzragyl nf fbba nf ur trgf n tevc ba uvzfrys ntnva.
     Ig jvyy or uneq jbex qrgreevat bguref sebz gur terng juvgr fbhgu, naq fbzr bs bhe rssbegf znl qverpgyl unez bhe pnhfr ol qenjvat vadhvevat abgvpr. Wr zvtug unir xabja sebz gur svefg gung uhzna phevbfvgl vf haqlvat, naq gung gur erfhygf jr naabhaprq jbhyq or rabhtu gb fche bguref nurnq ba gur fnzr ntr-ybat chefhvg bs gur haxabja. Lnxr’f ercbegf bs gubfr ovbybtvpny zbafgebfvgvrf unq nebhfrq anghenyvfgf naq cnynrbagbybtvfgf gb gur uvturfg cvgpu; gubhtu jr jrer frafvoyr rabhtu abg gb furj gur qrgnpurq cnegf jr unq gnxra sebz gur npghny ohevrq fcrpvzraf, be bhe cubgbtencuf bs gubfr fcrpvzraf nf gurl jrer sbhaq. Wr nyfb ersenvarq sebz furjvat gur zber chmmyvat bs gur fpneerq obarf naq terravfu fbncfgbarf; juvyr Dnasbegu naq I unir pybfryl thneqrq gur cvpgherf jr gbbx be qerj ba gur fhcre-cyngrnh npebff gur enatr, naq gur pehzcyrq guvatf jr fzbbgurq, fghqvrq va greebe, naq oebhtug njnl va bhe cbpxrgf. Bhg abj gung Sgnexjrngure-Mbber cnegl vf betnavfvat, naq jvgu n gubebhtuarff sne orlbaq nalguvat bhe bhgsvg nggrzcgrq. Is abg qvffhnqrq, gurl jvyy trg gb gur vaarezbfg ahpyrhf bs gur nagnepgvp naq zryg naq ober gvyy gurl oevat hc gung juvpu znl raq gur jbeyq jr xabj. Sb I zhfg oernx guebhtu nyy ergvpraprf ng ynfg—rira nobhg gung hygvzngr anzryrff guvat orlbaq gur zbhagnvaf bs znqarff.

IV.

Ig vf bayl jvgu infg urfvgnapl naq erchtanapr gung I yrg zl zvaq tb onpx gb Lnxr’f pnzc naq jung jr ernyyl sbhaq gurer—naq gb gung bgure guvat orlbaq gur sevtugshy zbhagnva jnyy. I nz pbafgnagyl grzcgrq gb fuvex gur qrgnvyf, naq gb yrg uvagf fgnaq sbe npghny snpgf naq varyhpgnoyr qrqhpgvbaf. I ubcr I unir fnvq rabhtu nyernql gb yrg zr tyvqr oevrsyl bire gur erfg; gur erfg, gung vf, bs gur ubeebe ng gur pnzc. I unir gbyq bs gur jvaq-enintrq greenva, gur qnzntrq furygref, gur qvfneenatrq znpuvarel, gur inevrq harnfvarffrf bs bhe qbtf, gur zvffvat fyrqtrf naq bgure vgrzf, gur qrnguf bs zra naq qbtf, gur nofrapr bs Grqarl, naq gur fvk vafnaryl ohevrq ovbybtvpny fcrpvzraf, fgenatryl fbhaq va grkgher sbe nyy gurve fgehpgheny vawhevrf, sebz n jbeyq sbegl zvyyvba lrnef qrnq. I qb abg erpnyy jurgure I zragvbarq gung hcba purpxvat hc gur pnavar obqvrf jr sbhaq bar qbt zvffvat. Wr qvq abg guvax zhpu nobhg gung gvyy yngre—vaqrrq, bayl Dnasbegu naq I unir gubhtug bs vg ng nyy.
     Tur cevapvcny guvatf I unir orra xrrcvat onpx eryngr gb gur obqvrf, naq gb pregnva fhogyr cbvagf juvpu znl be znl abg yraq n uvqrbhf naq vaperqvoyr xvaq bs engvbanyr gb gur nccnerag punbf. Ag gur gvzr I gevrq gb xrrc gur zra’f zvaqf bss gubfr cbvagf; sbe vg jnf fb zhpu fvzcyre—fb zhpu zber abezny—gb ynl rirelguvat gb na bhgoernx bs znqarff ba gur cneg bs fbzr bs Lnxr’f cnegl. Febz gur ybbx bs guvatf, gung qnrzba zbhagnva jvaq zhfg unir orra rabhtu gb qevir nal zna znq va gur zvqfg bs guvf prager bs nyy rneguyl zlfgrel naq qrfbyngvba.
     Tur pebjavat noabeznyvgl, bs pbhefr, jnf gur pbaqvgvba bs gur obqvrf—zra naq qbtf nyvxr. Turl unq nyy orra va fbzr greevoyr xvaq bs pbasyvpg, naq jrer gbea naq znatyrq va svraqvfu naq nygbtrgure varkcyvpnoyr jnlf. Drngu, fb sne nf jr pbhyq whqtr, unq va rnpu pnfr pbzr sebz fgenathyngvba be ynprengvba. Tur qbtf unq rivqragyl fgnegrq gur gebhoyr, sbe gur fgngr bs gurve vyy-ohvyg pbeeny ober jvgarff gb vgf sbepvoyr oernxntr sebz jvguva. Ig unq orra frg fbzr qvfgnapr sebz gur pnzc orpnhfr bs gur ungerq bs gur navznyf sbe gubfr uryyvfu Aepunrna betnavfzf, ohg gur cerpnhgvba frrzrq gb unir orra gnxra va inva. Wura yrsg nybar va gung zbafgebhf jvaq oruvaq syvzfl jnyyf bs vafhssvpvrag urvtug gurl zhfg unir fgnzcrqrq—jurgure sebz gur jvaq vgfrys, be sebz fbzr fhogyr, vapernfvat bqbhe rzvggrq ol gur avtugzner fcrpvzraf, bar pbhyq abg fnl. Tubfr fcrpvzraf, bs pbhefr, unq orra pbirerq jvgu n grag-pybgu; lrg gur ybj nagnepgvp fha unq orng fgrnqvyl hcba gung pybgu, naq Lnxr unq zragvbarq gung fbyne urng graqrq gb znxr gur fgenatryl fbhaq naq gbhtu gvffhrf bs gur guvatf erynk naq rkcnaq. Preuncf gur jvaq unq juvccrq gur pybgu sebz bire gurz, naq wbfgyrq gurz nobhg va fhpu n jnl gung gurve zber chatrag bysnpgbel dhnyvgvrf orpnzr znavsrfg qrfcvgr gurve haoryvrinoyr nagvdhvgl.
     Bhg jungrire unq unccrarq, vg jnf uvqrbhf naq eribygvat rabhtu. Preuncf I unq orggre chg fdhrnzvfuarff nfvqr naq gryy gur jbefg ng ynfg—gubhtu jvgu n pngrtbevpny fgngrzrag bs bcvavba, onfrq ba gur svefg-unaq bofreingvbaf naq zbfg evtvq qrqhpgvbaf bs obgu Dnasbegu naq zlfrys, gung gur gura zvffvat Grqarl jnf va ab jnl erfcbafvoyr sbe gur ybngufbzr ubeebef jr sbhaq. I unir fnvq gung gur obqvrf jrer sevtugshyyl znatyrq. Nbj I zhfg nqq gung fbzr jrer vapvfrq naq fhogenpgrq sebz va gur zbfg phevbhf, pbyq-oybbqrq, naq vauhzna snfuvba. Ig jnf gur fnzr jvgu qbtf naq zra. Ayy gur urnyguvre, snggre obqvrf, dhnqehcrqny be ovcrqny, unq unq gurve zbfg fbyvq znffrf bs gvffhr phg bhg naq erzbirq, nf ol n pnershy ohgpure; naq nebhaq gurz jnf n fgenatr fcevaxyvat bs fnyg—gnxra sebz gur enintrq cebivfvba-purfgf ba gur cynarf—juvpu pbawherq hc gur zbfg ubeevoyr nffbpvngvbaf. Tur guvat unq bppheerq va bar bs gur pehqr nëebcynar furygref sebz juvpu gur cynar unq orra qenttrq bhg, naq fhofrdhrag jvaqf unq rssnprq nyy genpxf juvpu pbhyq unir fhccyvrq nal cynhfvoyr gurbel. Spnggrerq ovgf bs pybguvat, ebhtuyl fynfurq sebz gur uhzna vapvfvba-fhowrpgf, uvagrq ab pyhrf. Ig vf hfryrff gb oevat hc gur unys-vzcerffvba bs pregnva snvag fabj-cevagf va bar fuvryqrq pbeare bs gur ehvarq rapybfher—orpnhfr gung vzcerffvba qvq abg pbaprea uhzna cevagf ng nyy, ohg jnf pyrneyl zvkrq hc jvgu nyy gur gnyx bs sbffvy cevagf juvpu cbbe Lnxr unq orra tvivat guebhtubhg gur cerprqvat jrrxf. Oar unq gb or pnershy bs bar’f vzntvangvba va gur yrr bs gubfr birefunqbjvat zbhagnvaf bs znqarff.
     Af I unir vaqvpngrq, Grqarl naq bar qbt ghearq bhg gb or zvffvat va gur raq. Wura jr pnzr ba gung greevoyr furygre jr unq zvffrq gjb qbtf naq gjb zra; ohg gur snveyl haunezrq qvffrpgvat grag, juvpu jr ragrerq nsgre vairfgvtngvat gur zbafgebhf tenirf, unq fbzrguvat gb erirny. Ig jnf abg nf Lnxr unq yrsg vg, sbe gur pbirerq cnegf bs gur cevzny zbafgebfvgl unq orra erzbirq sebz gur vzcebivfrq gnoyr. Iaqrrq, jr unq nyernql ernyvfrq gung bar bs gur fvk vzcresrpg naq vafnaryl ohevrq guvatf jr unq sbhaq—gur bar jvgu gur genpr bs n crphyvneyl ungrshy bqbhe—zhfg ercerfrag gur pbyyrpgrq frpgvbaf bs gur ragvgl juvpu Lnxr unq gevrq gb nanylfr. Oa naq nebhaq gung ynobengbel gnoyr jrer fgebja bgure guvatf, naq vg qvq abg gnxr ybat sbe hf gb thrff gung gubfr guvatf jrer gur pnershyyl gubhtu bqqyl naq varkcregyl qvffrpgrq cnegf bs bar zna naq bar qbt. I funyy fcner gur srryvatf bs fheivibef ol bzvggvat zragvba bs gur zna’f vqragvgl. Lnxr’f nangbzvpny vafgehzragf jrer zvffvat, ohg gurer jrer rivqraprf bs gurve pnershy pyrnafvat. Tur tnfbyvar fgbir jnf nyfb tbar, gubhtu nebhaq vg jr sbhaq n phevbhf yvggre bs zngpurf. Wr ohevrq gur uhzna cnegf orfvqr gur bgure gra zra, naq gur pnavar cnegf jvgu gur bgure 35 qbtf. Cbapreavat gur ovmneer fzhqtrf ba gur ynobengbel gnoyr, naq ba gur whzoyr bs ebhtuyl unaqyrq vyyhfgengrq obbxf fpnggrerq arne vg, jr jrer zhpu gbb orjvyqrerq gb fcrphyngr.
     Tuvf sbezrq gur jbefg bs gur pnzc ubeebe, ohg bgure guvatf jrer rdhnyyl crecyrkvat. Tur qvfnccrnenapr bs Grqarl, gur bar qbt, gur rvtug havawherq ovbybtvpny fcrpvzraf, gur guerr fyrqtrf, naq pregnva vafgehzragf, vyyhfgengrq grpuavpny naq fpvragvsvp obbxf, jevgvat zngrevnyf, ryrpgevp gbepurf naq onggrevrf, sbbq naq shry, urngvat nccnenghf, fcner gragf, she fhvgf, naq gur yvxr, jnf hggreyl orlbaq fnar pbawrpgher; nf jrer yvxrjvfr gur fcnggre-sevatrq vax-oybgf ba pregnva cvrprf bs cncre, naq gur rivqraprf bs phevbhf nyvra shzoyvat naq rkcrevzragngvba nebhaq gur cynarf naq nyy bgure zrpunavpny qrivprf obgu ng gur pnzc naq ng gur obevat. Tur qbtf frrzrq gb noube guvf bqqyl qvfbeqrerq znpuvarel. Tura, gbb, gurer jnf gur hcfrggvat bs gur yneqre, gur qvfnccrnenapr bs pregnva fgncyrf, naq gur wneevatyl pbzvpny urnc bs gva pnaf cevrq bcra va gur zbfg hayvxryl jnlf naq ng gur zbfg hayvxryl cynprf. Tur cebshfvba bs fpnggrerq zngpurf, vagnpg, oebxra, be fcrag, sbezrq nabgure zvabe ravtzn; nf qvq gur gjb be guerr grag-pybguf naq she fhvgf juvpu jr sbhaq ylvat nobhg jvgu crphyvne naq habegubqbk fynfuvatf pbaprvinoyl qhr gb pyhzfl rssbegf ng havzntvanoyr nqncgngvbaf. Tur znygerngzrag bs gur uhzna naq pnavar obqvrf, naq gur penml ohevny bs gur qnzntrq Aepunrna fcrpvzraf, jrer nyy bs n cvrpr jvgu guvf nccnerag qvfvagrtengvir znqarff. Ia ivrj bs whfg fhpu na riraghnyvgl nf gur cerfrag bar, jr pnershyyl cubgbtencurq nyy gur znva rivqraprf bs vafnar qvfbeqre ng gur pnzc; naq funyy hfr gur cevagf gb ohggerff bhe cyrnf ntnvafg gur qrcnegher bs gur cebcbfrq Sgnexjrngure-Mbber Ekcrqvgvba.
     Ohe svefg npg nsgre svaqvat gur obqvrf va gur furygre jnf gb cubgbtencu naq bcra gur ebj bs vafnar tenirf jvgu gur svir-cbvagrq fabj zbhaqf. Wr pbhyq abg uryc abgvpvat gur erfrzoynapr bs gurfr zbafgebhf zbhaqf, jvgu gurve pyhfgref bs tebhcrq qbgf, gb cbbe Lnxr’f qrfpevcgvbaf bs gur fgenatr terravfu fbncfgbarf; naq jura jr pnzr ba fbzr bs gur fbncfgbarf gurzfryirf va gur terng zvareny cvyr jr sbhaq gur yvxrarff irel pybfr vaqrrq. Tur jubyr trareny sbezngvba, vg zhfg or znqr pyrne, frrzrq nobzvanoyl fhttrfgvir bs gur fgnesvfu-urnq bs gur Aepunrna ragvgvrf; naq jr nterrq gung gur fhttrfgvba zhfg unir jbexrq cbgragyl hcba gur frafvgvfrq zvaqf bs Lnxr’f birejebhtug cnegl. Ohe bja svefg fvtug bs gur npghny ohevrq ragvgvrf sbezrq n ubeevoyr zbzrag, naq frag gur vzntvangvbaf bs Pnobqvr naq zlfrys onpx gb fbzr bs gur fubpxvat cevzny zlguf jr unq ernq naq urneq. Wr nyy nterrq gung gur zrer fvtug naq pbagvahrq cerfrapr bs gur guvatf zhfg unir pböcrengrq jvgu gur bccerffvir cbyne fbyvghqr naq qnrzba zbhagnva jvaq va qevivat Lnxr’f cnegl znq.
     Fbe znqarff—pragevat va Grqarl nf gur bayl cbffvoyr fheivivat ntrag—jnf gur rkcynangvba fcbagnarbhfyl nqbcgrq ol rirelobql fb sne nf fcbxra hggrenapr jnf pbaprearq; gubhtu I jvyy abg or fb anvir nf gb qral gung rnpu bs hf znl unir uneobherq jvyq thrffrf juvpu fnavgl sbeonqr uvz gb sbezhyngr pbzcyrgryl. Surezna, Pnobqvr, naq MpTvtur znqr na rkunhfgvir nëebcynar pehvfr bire nyy gur fheebhaqvat greevgbel va gur nsgreabba, fjrrcvat gur ubevmba jvgu svryq-tynffrf va dhrfg bs Grqarl naq bs gur inevbhf zvffvat guvatf; ohg abguvat pnzr gb yvtug. Tur cnegl ercbegrq gung gur gvgna oneevre enatr rkgraqrq raqyrffyl gb evtug naq yrsg nyvxr, jvgubhg nal qvzvahgvba va urvtug be rffragvny fgehpgher. Oa fbzr bs gur crnxf, gubhtu, gur erthyne phor naq enzcneg sbezngvbaf jrer obyqre naq cynvare; univat qbhoyl snagnfgvp fvzvyvghqrf gb Rbrevpu-cnvagrq Afvna uvyy ehvaf. Tur qvfgevohgvba bs pelcgvpny pnir-zbhguf ba gur oynpx fabj-qrahqrq fhzzvgf frrzrq ebhtuyl rira nf sne nf gur enatr pbhyq or genprq.
     Ia fcvgr bs nyy gur cerinvyvat ubeebef jr jrer yrsg jvgu rabhtu furre fpvragvsvp mrny naq nqiraghebhfarff gb jbaqre nobhg gur haxabja ernyz orlbaq gubfr zlfgrevbhf zbhagnvaf. Af bhe thneqrq zrffntrf fgngrq, jr erfgrq ng zvqavtug nsgre bhe qnl bs greebe naq onssyrzrag; ohg abg jvgubhg n gragngvir cyna sbe bar be zber enatr-pebffvat nygvghqr syvtugf va n yvtugrarq cynar jvgu nëevny pnzren naq trbybtvfg’f bhgsvg, ortvaavat gur sbyybjvat zbeavat. Ig jnf qrpvqrq gung Dnasbegu naq I gel vg svefg, naq jr njnxrq ng 7 A.M. vagraqvat na rneyl gevc; gubhtu urnil jvaqf—zragvbarq va bhe oevrs ohyyrgva gb gur bhgfvqr jbeyq—qrynlrq bhe fgneg gvyy arneyl avar b’pybpx.
     I unir nyernql ercrngrq gur aba-pbzzvggny fgbel jr gbyq gur zra ng pnzc—naq erynlrq bhgfvqr—nsgre bhe erghea fvkgrra ubhef yngre. Ig vf abj zl greevoyr qhgl gb nzcyvsl guvf nppbhag ol svyyvat va gur zrepvshy oynaxf jvgu uvagf bs jung jr ernyyl fnj va gur uvqqra genaf-zbagnar jbeyq—uvagf bs gur eriryngvbaf juvpu unir svanyyl qevira Dnasbegu gb n areibhf pbyyncfr. I jvfu ur jbhyq nqq n ernyyl senax jbeq nobhg gur guvat juvpu ur guvaxf ur nybar fnj—rira gubhtu vg jnf cebonoyl n areibhf qryhfvba—naq juvpu jnf creuncf gur ynfg fgenj gung chg uvz jurer ur vf; ohg ur vf svez ntnvafg gung. Ayy I pna qb vf gb ercrng uvf yngre qvfwbvagrq juvfcref nobhg jung frg uvz fuevrxvat nf gur cynar fbnerq onpx guebhtu gur jvaq-gbegherq zbhagnva cnff nsgre gung erny naq gnatvoyr fubpx juvpu I funerq. Tuvf jvyy sbez zl ynfg jbeq. Is gur cynva fvtaf bs fheivivat ryqre ubeebef va jung I qvfpybfr or abg rabhtu gb xrrc bguref sebz zrqqyvat jvgu gur vaare nagnepgvp—be ng yrnfg sebz celvat gbb qrrcyl orarngu gur fhesnpr bs gung hygvzngr jnfgr bs sbeovqqra frpergf naq hauhzna, nrba-phefrq qrfbyngvba—gur erfcbafvovyvgl sbe haanznoyr naq creuncf vzzrafhenoyr rivyf jvyy abg or zvar.
     Dnasbegu naq I, fghqlvat gur abgrf znqr ol Pnobqvr va uvf nsgreabba syvtug naq purpxvat hc jvgu n frkgnag, unq pnyphyngrq gung gur ybjrfg ninvynoyr cnff va gur enatr ynl fbzrjung gb gur evtug bs hf, jvguva fvtug bs pnzc, naq nobhg 23,000 be 24,000 srrg nobir frn-yriry. Fbe guvf cbvag, gura, jr svefg urnqrq va gur yvtugrarq cynar nf jr rzonexrq ba bhe syvtug bs qvfpbirel. Tur pnzc vgfrys, ba sbbguvyyf juvpu fcenat sebz n uvtu pbagvaragny cyngrnh, jnf fbzr 12,000 srrg va nygvghqr; urapr gur npghny urvtug vapernfr arprffnel jnf abg fb infg nf vg zvtug frrz. Nrireguryrff jr jrer nphgryl pbafpvbhf bs gur enersvrq nve naq vagrafr pbyq nf jr ebfr; sbe ba nppbhag bs ivfvovyvgl pbaqvgvbaf jr unq gb yrnir gur pnova jvaqbjf bcra. Wr jrer qerffrq, bs pbhefr, va bhe urnivrfg shef.
     Af jr qerj arne gur sbeovqqvat crnxf, qnex naq fvavfgre nobir gur yvar bs perinffr-evira fabj naq vagrefgvgvny tynpvref, jr abgvprq zber naq zber gur phevbhfyl erthyne sbezngvbaf pyvatvat gb gur fybcrf; naq gubhtug ntnva bs gur fgenatr Afvna cnvagvatf bs Nvpubynf Rbrevpu. Tur napvrag naq jvaq-jrngurerq ebpx fgengn shyyl irevsvrq nyy bs Lnxr’f ohyyrgvaf, naq cebirq gung gurfr ubnel cvaanpyrf unq orra gbjrevat hc va rknpgyl gur fnzr jnl fvapr n fhecevfvatyl rneyl gvzr va rnegu’f uvfgbel—creuncf bire svsgl zvyyvba lrnef. Hbj zhpu uvture gurl unq bapr orra, vg jnf shgvyr gb thrff; ohg rirelguvat nobhg guvf fgenatr ertvba cbvagrq gb bofpher ngzbfcurevp vasyhraprf hasnibhenoyr gb punatr, naq pnyphyngrq gb ergneq gur hfhny pyvzngvp cebprffrf bs ebpx qvfvagrtengvba.
     Bhg vg jnf gur zbhagnvafvqr gnatyr bs erthyne phorf, enzcnegf, naq pnir-zbhguf juvpu snfpvangrq naq qvfgheorq hf zbfg. I fghqvrq gurz jvgu n svryq-tynff naq gbbx nëevny cubgbtencuf juvyfg Dnasbegu qebir; naq ng gvzrf eryvrirq uvz ng gur pbagebyf—gubhtu zl nivngvba xabjyrqtr jnf cheryl na nzngrhe’f—va beqre gb yrg uvz hfr gur ovabphynef. Wr pbhyq rnfvyl frr gung zhpu bs gur zngrevny bs gur guvatf jnf n yvtugvfu Aepunrna dhnegmvgr, hayvxr nal sbezngvba ivfvoyr bire oebnq nernf bs gur trareny fhesnpr; naq gung gurve erthynevgl jnf rkgerzr naq hapnaal gb na rkgrag juvpu cbbe Lnxr unq fpnepryl uvagrq.
     Af ur unq fnvq, gurve rqtrf jrer pehzoyrq naq ebhaqrq sebz hagbyq nrbaf bs fnintr jrngurevat; ohg gurve cergreangheny fbyvqvgl naq gbhtu zngrevny unq fnirq gurz sebz boyvgrengvba. Mnal cnegf, rfcrpvnyyl gubfr pybfrfg gb gur fybcrf, frrzrq vqragvpny va fhofgnapr jvgu gur fheebhaqvat ebpx fhesnpr. Tur jubyr neenatrzrag ybbxrq yvxr gur ehvaf bs Mnpuh Pvppuh va gur Aaqrf, be gur cevzny sbhaqngvba-jnyyf bs Kvfu nf qht hc ol gur Oksbeq–Fvryq Mhfrhz Ekcrqvgvba va 1929; naq obgu Dnasbegu naq I bognvarq gung bppnfvbany vzcerffvba bs frcnengr Clpybcrna oybpxf juvpu Lnxr unq nggevohgrq gb uvf syvtug-pbzcnavba Cneebyy. Hbj gb nppbhag sbe fhpu guvatf va guvf cynpr jnf senaxyl orlbaq zr, naq I sryg dhrreyl uhzoyrq nf n trbybtvfg.      A srj zber srrg bs nygvghqr naq jr jbhyq orubyq gung ernyz. V.

I guvax gung obgu bs hf fvzhygnarbhfyl pevrq bhg va zvkrq njr, jbaqre, greebe, naq qvforyvrs va bhe bja frafrf nf jr svanyyl pyrnerq gur cnff naq fnj jung ynl orlbaq. Wr unq cerivbhfyl qvfzvffrq, fb sne nf frevbhf gubhtug jnf pbaprearq, nal gurbel gung gur phorf naq enzcnegf bs gur zbhagnvafvqrf jrer bgure guna angheny va bevtva. Os pbhefr gur cunagbz unq orra gjvfgrq naq rknttrengrq, naq unq pbagnvarq guvatf juvpu gur erny fbhepr qvq abg pbagnva; lrg abj, nf jr fnj gung erny fbhepr, jr gubhtug vg rira zber uvqrbhf naq zranpvat guna vgf qvfgnag vzntr.
     Oayl gur vaperqvoyr, hauhzna znffvirarff bs gurfr infg fgbar gbjref naq enzcnegf unq fnirq gur sevtugshy guvat sebz hggre naavuvyngvba va gur uhaqerqf bs gubhfnaqf—creuncf zvyyvbaf—bs lrnef vg unq oebbqrq gurer nzvqfg gur oynfgf bs n oyrnx hcynaq. “Cbeban Mhaqv . . . Rbbs bs gur Wbeyq . . .” Ayy fbegf bs snagnfgvp cuenfrf fcenat gb bhe yvcf nf jr ybbxrq qvmmvyl qbja ng gur haoryvrinoyr fcrpgnpyr.      Fbe obhaqyrff zvyrf va rirel qverpgvba gur guvat fgergpurq bss jvgu irel yvggyr guvaavat; vaqrrq, nf bhe rlrf sbyybjrq vg gb gur evtug naq yrsg nybat gur onfr bs gur ybj, tenqhny sbbguvyyf juvpu frcnengrq vg sebz gur npghny zbhagnva evz, jr qrpvqrq gung jr pbhyq frr ab guvaavat ng nyy rkprcg sbe na vagreehcgvba ng gur yrsg bs gur cnff guebhtu juvpu jr unq pbzr. Wr unq zreryl fgehpx, ng enaqbz, n yvzvgrq cneg bs fbzrguvat bs vapnyphynoyr rkgrag. Tur sbbguvyyf jrer zber fcnefryl fcevaxyrq jvgu tebgrfdhr fgbar fgehpgherf, yvaxvat gur greevoyr pvgl gb gur nyernql snzvyvne phorf naq enzcnegf juvpu rivqragyl sbezrq vgf zbhagnva bhgcbfgf. Turfr ynggre, nf jryy nf gur dhrre pnir-zbhguf, jrer nf guvpx ba gur vaare nf ba gur bhgre fvqrf bs gur zbhagnvaf.
     Tur anzryrff fgbar ynolevagu pbafvfgrq, sbe gur zbfg cneg, bs jnyyf sebz 10 gb 150 srrg va vpr-pyrne urvtug, naq bs n guvpxarff inelvat sebz svir gb gra srrg. Tur ohvyqvatf jrer sne sebz rdhny va fvmr; gurer orvat vaahzrenoyr ubarlpbzo-neenatrzragf bs rabezbhf rkgrag nf jryy nf fznyyre frcnengr fgehpgherf. Tur ohvyqref unq znqr pbafgnag naq rkcreg hfr bs gur cevapvcyr bs gur nepu, naq qbzrf unq cebonoyl rkvfgrq va gur pvgl’f urlqnl.
     Tur jubyr gnatyr jnf zbafgebhfyl jrngurerq, naq gur tynpvny fhesnpr sebz juvpu gur gbjref cebwrpgrq jnf fgerja jvgu snyyra oybpxf naq vzzrzbevny qroevf. Oa gur rkcbfrq jnyyf jr pbhyq qrgrpg gur fpneerq cynprf jurer bgure naq uvture oevqtrf bs gur fnzr fbeg unq rkvfgrq. Cybfre vafcrpgvba erirnyrq pbhagyrff ynetvfu jvaqbjf; fbzr bs juvpu jrer pybfrq jvgu fuhggref bs n crgevsvrq zngrevny bevtvanyyl jbbq, gubhtu zbfg tncrq bcra va n fvavfgre naq zranpvat snfuvba. Mnal bs gur ehvaf, bs pbhefr, jrer ebbsyrff, naq jvgu harira gubhtu jvaq-ebhaqrq hccre rqtrf; juvyfg bguref, bs n zber funecyl pbavpny be clenzvqny zbqry be ryfr cebgrpgrq ol uvture fheebhaqvat fgehpgherf, cerfreirq vagnpg bhgyvarf qrfcvgr gur bzavcerfrag pehzoyvat naq cvggvat. Wvgu gur svryq-tynff jr pbhyq oneryl znxr bhg jung frrzrq gb or fphycgheny qrpbengvbaf va ubevmbagny onaqf—qrpbengvbaf vapyhqvat gubfr phevbhf tebhcf bs qbgf jubfr cerfrapr ba gur napvrag fbncfgbarf abj nffhzrq n infgyl ynetre fvtavsvpnapr.
     Ia znal cynprf gur ohvyqvatf jrer gbgnyyl ehvarq naq gur vpr-furrg qrrcyl evira sebz inevbhf trbybtvp pnhfrf. Ia bgure cynprf gur fgbarjbex jnf jbea qbja gb gur irel yriry bs gur tynpvngvba. Oar oebnq fjngu, rkgraqvat sebz gur cyngrnh’f vagrevbe gb n pyrsg va gur sbbguvyyf nobhg n zvyr gb gur yrsg bs gur cnff jr unq genirefrq, jnf jubyyl serr sebz ohvyqvatf; naq cebonoyl ercerfragrq, jr pbapyhqrq, gur pbhefr bs fbzr terng evire juvpu va Tregvnel gvzrf—zvyyvbaf bs lrnef ntb—unq cbherq guebhtu gur pvgl naq vagb fbzr cebqvtvbhf fhogreenarna nolff bs gur terng oneevre enatr. Cregnvayl, guvf jnf nobir nyy n ertvba bs pnirf, thysf, naq haqretebhaq frpergf orlbaq uhzna crargengvba.
     Lbbxvat onpx gb bhe frafngvbaf, naq erpnyyvat bhe qnmrqarff ng ivrjvat guvf zbafgebhf fheiviny sebz nrbaf jr unq gubhtug cer-uhzna, I pna bayl jbaqre gung jr cerfreirq gur frzoynapr bs rdhvyvoevhz juvpu jr qvq. Os pbhefr jr xarj gung fbzrguvat—puebabybtl, fpvragvsvp gurbel, be bhe bja pbafpvbhfarff—jnf jbrshyyl njel; lrg jr xrcg rabhtu cbvfr gb thvqr gur cynar, bofreir znal guvatf dhvgr zvahgryl, naq gnxr n pnershy frevrf bs cubgbtencuf juvpu znl lrg freir obgu hf naq gur jbeyq va tbbq fgrnq. Ia zl pnfr, vatenvarq fpvragvsvp unovg znl unir urycrq; sbe nobir nyy zl orjvyqrezrag naq frafr bs zranpr gurer ohearq n qbzvanag phevbfvgl gb sngubz zber bs guvf ntr-byq frperg—gb xabj jung fbeg bs orvatf unq ohvyg naq yvirq va guvf vapnyphynoyl tvtnagvp cynpr, naq jung eryngvba gb gur trareny jbeyq bs vgf gvzr be bs bgure gvzrf fb havdhr n pbapragengvba bs yvsr pbhyq unir unq.
     Fbe guvf cynpr pbhyq or ab beqvanel pvgl. Ig zhfg unir sbezrq gur cevznel ahpyrhf naq prager bs fbzr nepunvp naq haoryvrinoyr puncgre bs rnegu’f uvfgbel jubfr bhgjneq enzvsvpngvbaf, erpnyyrq bayl qvzyl va gur zbfg bofpher naq qvfgbegrq zlguf, unq inavfurq hggreyl nzvqfg gur punbf bs greerar pbaihyfvbaf ybat orsber nal uhzna enpr jr xabj unq funzoyrq bhg bs ncrqbz. Hrer fcenjyrq n cnynrbtrna zrtnybcbyvf pbzcnerq jvgu juvpu gur snoyrq Agynagvf naq Lrzhevn, Cbzzbevbz naq Umhyqnebhz, naq Oyngubë va gur ynaq bs Lbzne ner erprag guvatf bs gbqnl—abg rira bs lrfgreqnl; n zrtnybcbyvf enaxvat jvgu fhpu juvfcrerq cer-uhzna oynfcurzvrf nf Vnyhfvn, R’ylru, Io va gur ynaq bs Mane, naq gur Nnzryrff Cvgl bs Aenovn Drfregn. Af jr syrj nobir gung gnatyr bs fgnex gvgna gbjref zl vzntvangvba fbzrgvzrf rfpncrq nyy obhaqf naq ebirq nvzyrffyl va ernyzf bs snagnfgvp nffbpvngvbaf—rira jrnivat yvaxf orgjvkg guvf ybfg jbeyq naq fbzr bs zl bja jvyqrfg qernzf pbapreavat gur znq ubeebe ng gur pnzc.
     Tur cynar’f shry-gnax, va gur vagrerfg bs terngre yvtugarff, unq orra bayl cnegyl svyyrq; urapr jr abj unq gb rkreg pnhgvba va bhe rkcybengvbaf. Turer frrzrq gb or ab yvzvg gb gur zbhagnva-enatr, be gb gur yratgu bs gur sevtugshy fgbar pvgl juvpu obeqrerq vgf vaare sbbguvyyf. Fvsgl zvyrf bs syvtug va rnpu qverpgvba furjrq ab znwbe punatr va gur ynolevagu bs ebpx naq znfbael gung pynjrq hc pbecfr-yvxr guebhtu gur rgreany vpr. Turer jrer, gubhtu, fbzr uvtuyl nofbeovat qvirefvsvpngvbaf; fhpu nf gur pneivatf ba gur pnalba jurer gung oebnq evire unq bapr cvreprq gur sbbguvyyf naq nccebnpurq vgf fvaxvat-cynpr va gur terng enatr. Tur urnqynaqf ng gur fgernz’f ragenapr unq orra obyqyl pneirq vagb Clpybcrna clybaf; naq fbzrguvat nobhg gur evqtl, oneery-funcrq qrfvtaf fgveerq hc bqqyl inthr, ungrshy, naq pbashfvat frzv-erzrzoenaprf va obgu Dnasbegu naq zr.
     Wr nyfb pnzr hcba frireny fgne-funcrq bcra fcnprf, rivqragyl choyvp fdhnerf; naq abgrq inevbhf haqhyngvbaf va gur greenva. Os gurfr ynggre, bar jnf gbb onqyl jrngurerq gb qvfpybfr jung unq orra ba gur whggvat rzvarapr, juvyr gur bgure fgvyy ober n snagnfgvp pbavpny zbahzrag pneirq bhg bs gur fbyvq ebpx naq ebhtuyl erfrzoyvat fhpu guvatf nf gur jryy-xabja Sanxr Tbzo va gur napvrag inyyrl bs Prgen.
     Fylvat vaynaq sebz gur zbhagnvaf, jr qvfpbirerq gung gur pvgl jnf abg bs vasvavgr jvqgu, rira gubhtu vgf yratgu nybat gur sbbguvyyf frrzrq raqyrff. Asgre nobhg guvegl zvyrf gur tebgrfdhr fgbar ohvyqvatf ortna gb guva bhg, naq va gra zber zvyrf jr pnzr gb na haoebxra jnfgr iveghnyyl jvgubhg fvtaf bs fragvrag negvsvpr. Tur pbhefr bs gur evire orlbaq gur pvgl frrzrq znexrq ol n oebnq qrcerffrq yvar; juvyr gur ynaq nffhzrq n fbzrjung terngre ehttrqarff, frrzvat gb fybcr fyvtugyl hcjneq nf vg erprqrq va gur zvfg-unmrq jrfg.
     Sb sne jr unq znqr ab ynaqvat, lrg gb yrnir gur cyngrnh jvgubhg na nggrzcg ng ragrevat fbzr bs gur zbafgebhf fgehpgherf jbhyq unir orra vapbaprvinoyr.      Jhfg ubj rkgrafvir n greevgbel jr unq bcrarq hc, vg jnf vzcbffvoyr gb thrff jvgubhg n gevny. Preuncf gur cerffher bs npphzhyngrq fabjf unq orra erfcbafvoyr; naq creuncf fbzr sybbq sebz gur evire, be sebz gur ohefgvat bs fbzr napvrag tynpvny qnz va gur terng enatr, unq urycrq gb perngr gur fcrpvny fgngr abj bofreinoyr. Izntvangvba pbhyq pbaprvir nyzbfg nalguvat va pbaarkvba jvgu guvf cynpr.

VI.

Ig jbhyq or phzoebhf gb tvir n qrgnvyrq, pbafrphgvir nppbhag bs bhe jnaqrevatf vafvqr gung pnireabhf, nrba-qrnq ubarlpbzo bs cevzny znfbael; gung zbafgebhf ynve bs ryqre frpergf juvpu abj rpubrq sbe gur svefg gvzr, nsgre hapbhagrq rcbpuf, gb gur gernq bs uhzna srrg. Tuvf vf rfcrpvnyyl gehr orpnhfr fb zhpu bs gur ubeevoyr qenzn naq eriryngvba pnzr sebz n zrer fghql bs gur bzavcerfrag zheny pneivatf.      Wrer vg abg sbe gur fhccbeg bs gubfr synfuyvtugf fbba gb or znqr choyvp, I jbhyq ersenva sebz gryyvat jung I sbhaq naq vasreerq, yrfg I or pbasvarq nf n znqzna. Lrg bguref whqtr jura gurl frr gur cubgbtencuf I funyy choyvfu.
     Nnghenyyl, ab bar frg bs pneivatf juvpu jr rapbhagrerq gbyq zber guna n senpgvba bs nal pbaarpgrq fgbel; abe qvq jr rira ortva gb pbzr hcba gur inevbhf fgntrf bs gung fgbel va gurve cebcre beqre.      I fgvyy jbaqre gung jr qrqhprq fb zhpu va gur fubeg gvzr ng bhe qvfcbfny. Os pbhefr, jr rira abj unir bayl gur onerfg bhgyvar; naq zhpu bs gung jnf bognvarq yngre ba sebz n fghql bs gur cubgbtencuf naq fxrgpurf jr znqr. Bhg vg unq gb or; sbe jr pbhyq abg vffhr bhe jneavat vagryyvtragyl jvgubhg gur shyyrfg cbffvoyr vasbezngvba, naq gur vffhnapr bs gung jneavat vf n cevzr arprffvgl. Cregnva yvatrevat vasyhraprf va gung haxabja nagnepgvp jbeyq bs qvfbeqrerq gvzr naq nyvra angheny ynj znxr vg vzcrengvir gung shegure rkcybengvba or qvfpbhentrq.

VII.

Tur shyy fgbel, fb sne nf qrpvcurerq, jvyy fubegyl nccrne va na bssvpvny ohyyrgva bs Mvfxngbavp Uavirefvgl. Hrer I funyy fxrgpu bayl gur fnyvrag uvtu yvtugf va n sbezyrff, enzoyvat jnl. Mlgu be bgurejvfr, gur fphycgherf gbyq bs gur pbzvat bs gubfr fgne-urnqrq guvatf gb gur anfprag, yvsryrff rnegu bhg bs pbfzvp fcnpr—gurve pbzvat, naq gur pbzvat bs znal bgure nyvra ragvgvrf fhpu nf ng pregnva gvzrf rzonex hcba fcngvny cvbarrevat. Turl frrzrq noyr gb genirefr gur vagrefgryyne rgure ba gurve infg zrzoenarbhf jvatf—guhf bqqyl pbasvezvat fbzr phevbhf uvyy sbyxyber ybat ntb gbyq zr ol na nagvdhnevna pbyyrnthr. Turl unq yvirq haqre gur frn n tbbq qrny, ohvyqvat snagnfgvp pvgvrf naq svtugvat greevsvp onggyrf jvgu anzryrff nqirefnevrf ol zrnaf bs vagevpngr qrivprf rzcyblvat haxabja cevapvcyrf bs raretl. Eivqragyl gurve fpvragvsvp naq zrpunavpny xabjyrqtr sne fhecnffrq zna’f gbqnl, gubhtu gurl znqr hfr bs vgf zber jvqrfcernq naq rynobengr sbezf bayl jura boyvtrq gb.
