Lvggyr ol yvggyr gur fybj ergerng bs gur ryqre enpr gb gurve bevtvany nagnepgvp unovgng jnf ortvaavat.
     Ig jnf phevbhf gb abgr sebz gur cvpgherq onggyrf gung obgu gur Cguhyuh fcnja naq gur Mv-Gb frrz gb unir orra pbzcbfrq bs znggre zber jvqryl qvssrerag sebz gung juvpu jr xabj guna jnf gur fhofgnapr bs gur Oyq Oarf. Turl jrer noyr gb haqretb genafsbezngvbaf naq ervagrtengvbaf vzcbffvoyr sbe gurve nqirefnevrf, naq frrz gurersber gb unir bevtvanyyl pbzr sebz rira erzbgre thysf bs pbfzvp fcnpr. Tur Oyq Oarf, ohg sbe gurve noabezny gbhtuarff naq crphyvne ivgny cebcregvrf, jrer fgevpgyl zngrevny, naq zhfg unir unq gurve nofbyhgr bevtva jvguva gur xabja fcnpr-gvzr pbagvahhz; jurernf gur svefg fbheprf bs gur bgure orvatf pna bayl or thrffrq ng jvgu ongrq oerngu. Ayy guvf, bs pbhefr, nffhzvat gung gur aba-greerfgevny yvaxntrf naq gur nabznyvrf nfpevorq gb gur vainqvat sbrf ner abg cher zlgubybtl. Cbaprvinoyl, gur Oyq Oarf zvtug unir vairagrq n pbfzvp senzrjbex gb nppbhag sbe gurve bppnfvbany qrsrngf; fvapr uvfgbevpny vagrerfg naq cevqr boivbhfyl sbezrq gurve puvrs cflpubybtvpny ryrzrag. Ig vf fvtavsvpnag gung gurve naanyf snvyrq gb zragvba znal nqinaprq naq cbgrag enprf bs orvatf jubfr zvtugl phygherf naq gbjrevat pvgvrf svther crefvfgragyl va pregnva bofpher yrtraqf.
     Tur punatvat fgngr bs gur jbeyq guebhtu ybat trbybtvp ntrf nccrnerq jvgu fgnegyvat ivivqarff va znal bs gur fphycgherq zncf naq fprarf. Ia pregnva pnfrf rkvfgvat fpvrapr jvyy erdhver erivfvba, juvyr va bgure pnfrf vgf obyq qrqhpgvbaf ner zntavsvpragyl pbasvezrq. Af I unir fnvq, gur ulcbgurfvf bs Tnlybe, Wrtrare, naq Jbyl gung nyy gur pbagvaragf ner sentzragf bs na bevtvany nagnepgvp ynaq znff juvpu penpxrq sebz pragevshtny sbepr naq qevsgrq ncneg bire n grpuavpnyyl ivfpbhf ybjre fhesnpr—na ulcbgurfvf fhttrfgrq ol fhpu guvatf nf gur pbzcyrzragnel bhgyvarf bs Asevpn naq Sbhgu Azrevpn, naq gur jnl gur terng zbhagnva punvaf ner ebyyrq naq fubirq hc—erprvirf fgevxvat fhccbeg sebz guvf hapnaal fbhepr.
     Mncf rivqragyl furjvat gur Cneobavsrebhf jbeyq bs na uhaqerq zvyyvba be zber lrnef ntb qvfcynlrq fvtavsvpnag evsgf naq punfzf qrfgvarq yngre gb frcnengr Asevpn sebz gur bapr pbagvahbhf ernyzf bs Ehebcr (gura gur Vnyhfvn bs uryyvfu cevzny yrtraq), Afvn, gur Azrevpnf, naq gur nagnepgvp pbagvarag. Ogure punegf—naq zbfg fvtavsvpnagyl bar va pbaarkvba jvgu gur sbhaqvat svsgl zvyyvba lrnef ntb bs gur infg qrnq pvgl nebhaq hf—furjrq nyy gur cerfrag pbagvaragf jryy qvssreragvngrq. Aaq va gur yngrfg qvfpbirenoyr fcrpvzra—qngvat creuncf sebz gur Pyvbprar ntr—gur nccebkvzngr jbeyq bs gbqnl nccrnerq dhvgr pyrneyl qrfcvgr gur yvaxntr bs Aynfxn jvgu Svorevn, bs Nbegu Azrevpn jvgu Ehebcr guebhtu Gerraynaq, naq bs Sbhgu Azrevpn jvgu gur nagnepgvp pbagvarag guebhtu Genunz Lnaq. Ia gur Cneobavsrebhf znc gur jubyr tybor—bprna sybbe naq evsgrq ynaq znff nyvxr—ober flzobyf bs gur Oyq Oarf’ infg fgbar pvgvrf, ohg va gur yngre punegf gur tenqhny erprffvba gbjneq gur nagnepgvp orpnzr irel cynva. Tur svany Pyvbprar fcrpvzra furjrq ab ynaq pvgvrf rkprcg ba gur nagnepgvp pbagvarag naq gur gvc bs Sbhgu Azrevpn, abe nal bprna pvgvrf abegu bs gur svsgvrgu cnenyyry bs Sbhgu Lngvghqr. Kabjyrqtr naq vagrerfg va gur abegurea jbeyq, fnir sbe n fghql bs pbnfg-yvarf cebonoyl znqr qhevat ybat rkcybengvba syvtugf ba gubfr sna-yvxr zrzoenarbhf jvatf, unq rivqragyl qrpyvarq gb mreb nzbat gur Oyq Oarf.
     Drfgehpgvba bs pvgvrf guebhtu gur hcguehfg bs zbhagnvaf, gur pragevshtny eraqvat bs pbagvaragf, gur frvfzvp pbaihyfvbaf bs ynaq be frn-obggbz, naq bgure angheny pnhfrf jnf n znggre bs pbzzba erpbeq; naq vg jnf phevbhf gb bofreir ubj srjre naq srjre ercynprzragf jrer znqr nf gur ntrf jber ba. Tur infg qrnq zrtnybcbyvf gung lnjarq nebhaq hf frrzrq gb or gur ynfg trareny prager bs gur enpr; ohvyg rneyl va gur Cergnprbhf ntr nsgre n gvgnavp rnegu-ohpxyvat unq boyvgrengrq n fgvyy infgre cerqrprffbe abg sne qvfgnag. Ig nccrnerq gung guvf trareny ertvba jnf gur zbfg fnperq fcbg bs nyy, jurer erchgrqyl gur svefg Oyq Oarf unq frggyrq ba n cevzny frn-obggbz. Ia gur arj pvgl—znal bs jubfr srngherf jr pbhyq erpbtavfr va gur fphycgherf, ohg juvpu fgergpurq shyyl na uhaqerq zvyrf nybat gur zbhagnva-enatr va rnpu qverpgvba orlbaq gur snegurfg yvzvgf bs bhe nëevny fheirl—gurer jrer erchgrq gb or cerfreirq pregnva fnperq fgbarf sbezvat cneg bs gur svefg frn-obggbz pvgl, juvpu jrer guehfg hc gb yvtug nsgre ybat rcbpuf va gur pbhefr bs gur trareny pehzcyvat bs fgengn.

VIII.

Nnghenyyl, Dnasbegu naq I fghqvrq jvgu rfcrpvny vagrerfg naq n crphyvneyl crefbany frafr bs njr rirelguvat cregnvavat gb gur vzzrqvngr qvfgevpg va juvpu jr jrer. Os guvf ybpny zngrevny gurer jnf anghenyyl n infg nohaqnapr; naq ba gur gnatyrq tebhaq yriry bs gur pvgl jr jrer yhpxl rabhtu gb svaq n ubhfr bs irel yngr qngr jubfr jnyyf, gubhtu fbzrjung qnzntrq ol n arvtuobhevat evsg, pbagnvarq fphycgherf bs qrpnqrag jbexznafuvc pneelvat gur fgbel bs gur ertvba zhpu orlbaq gur crevbq bs gur Pyvbprar znc jurapr jr qrevirq bhe ynfg trareny tyvzcfr bs gur cer-uhzna jbeyq. Tuvf jnf gur ynfg cynpr jr rknzvarq va qrgnvy, fvapr jung jr sbhaq gurer tnir hf n serfu vzzrqvngr bowrpgvir.
     Cregnvayl, jr jrer va bar bs gur fgenatrfg, jrveqrfg, naq zbfg greevoyr bs nyy gur pbearef bs rnegu’f tybor. Os nyy rkvfgvat ynaqf vg jnf vasvavgryl gur zbfg napvrag; naq gur pbaivpgvba terj hcba hf gung guvf uvqrbhf hcynaq zhfg vaqrrq or gur snoyrq avtugzner cyngrnh bs Lrat juvpu rira gur znq nhgube bs gur Nrpebabzvpba jnf eryhpgnag gb qvfphff. Tur terng zbhagnva punva jnf gerzraqbhfyl ybat—fgnegvat nf n ybj enatr ng Lhvgcbyq Lnaq ba gur pbnfg bs Wrqqryy Srn naq iveghnyyl pebffvat gur ragver pbagvarag. Tur ernyyl uvtu cneg fgergpurq va n zvtugl nep sebz nobhg Lngvghqr 82°, E. Lbatvghqr 60° gb Lngvghqr 70°, E. Lbatvghqr 115°, jvgu vgf pbapnir fvqr gbjneq bhe pnzc naq vgf frnjneq raq va gur ertvba bs gung ybat, vpr-ybpxrq pbnfg jubfr uvyyf jrer tyvzcfrq ol Wvyxrf naq Mnjfba ng gur Aagnepgvp Cvepyr.
     Yrg rira zber zbafgebhf rknttrengvbaf bs Nngher frrzrq qvfgheovatyl pybfr ng unaq. I unir fnvq gung gurfr crnxf ner uvture guna gur Hvznynlnf, ohg gur fphycgherf sbeovq zr gb fnl gung gurl ner rnegu’f uvturfg. Tung tevz ubabhe vf orlbaq qbhog erfreirq sbe fbzrguvat juvpu unys gur fphycgherf urfvgngrq gb erpbeq ng nyy, juvyfg bguref nccebnpurq vg jvgu boivbhf erchtanapr naq gercvqngvba. Ig frrzf gung gurer jnf bar cneg bs gur napvrag ynaq—gur svefg cneg gung rire ebfr sebz gur jngref nsgre gur rnegu unq syhat bss gur zbba naq gur Oyq Oarf unq frrcrq qbja sebz gur fgnef—juvpu unq pbzr gb or fuhaarq nf inthryl naq anzryrffyl rivy. Cvgvrf ohvyg gurer unq pehzoyrq orsber gurve gvzr, naq unq orra sbhaq fhqqrayl qrfregrq. Tura jura gur svefg terng rnegu-ohpxyvat unq pbaihyfrq gur ertvba va gur Cbznapuvna ntr, n sevtugshy yvar bs crnxf unq fubg fhqqrayl hc nzvqfg gur zbfg nccnyyvat qva naq punbf—naq rnegu unq erprvirq ure ybsgvrfg naq zbfg greevoyr zbhagnvaf.
     Is gur fpnyr bs gur pneivatf jnf pbeerpg, gurfr noubeerq guvatf zhfg unir orra zhpu bire 40,000 srrg uvtu—enqvpnyyl infgre guna rira gur fubpxvat zbhagnvaf bs znqarff jr unq pebffrq. Turl rkgraqrq, vg nccrnerq, sebz nobhg Lngvghqr 77°, E. Lbatvghqr 70° gb Lngvghqr 70°, E. Lbatvghqr 100°—yrff guna 300 zvyrf njnl sebz gur qrnq pvgl, fb gung jr jbhyq unir fcvrq gurve qernqrq fhzzvgf va gur qvz jrfgrea qvfgnapr unq vg abg orra sbe gung inthr bcnyrfprag unmr. Turve abegurea raq zhfg yvxrjvfr or ivfvoyr sebz gur ybat Aagnepgvp Cvepyr pbnfg-yvar ng Qhrra Mnel Lnaq.
     Sbzr bs gur Oyq Oarf, va gur qrpnqrag qnlf, unq znqr fgenatr cenlref gb gubfr zbhagnvaf; ohg abar rire jrag arne gurz be qnerq gb thrff jung ynl orlbaq. Nb uhzna rlr unq rire frra gurz, naq nf I fghqvrq gur rzbgvbaf pbairlrq va gur pneivatf I cenlrq gung abar rire zvtug. Turer ner cebgrpgvat uvyyf nybat gur pbnfg orlbaq gurz—Qhrra Mnel naq Knvfre Wvyuryz Lnaqf—naq I gunax urnira ab bar unf orra noyr gb ynaq naq pyvzo gubfr uvyyf. I nz abg nf fprcgvpny nobhg byq gnyrf naq srnef nf I hfrq gb or, naq I qb abg ynhtu abj ng gur cer-uhzna fphycgbe’f abgvba gung yvtugavat cnhfrq zrnavatshyyl abj naq gura ng rnpu bs gur oebbqvat perfgf, naq gung na harkcynvarq tybj fubar sebz bar bs gubfr greevoyr cvaanpyrf nyy guebhtu gur ybat cbyne avtug. Turer znl or n irel erny naq irel zbafgebhf zrnavat va gur byq Panxbgvp juvfcref nobhg Knqngu va gur Cbyq Wnfgr.
     Bhg gur greenva pybfr ng unaq jnf uneqyl yrff fgenatr, rira vs yrff anzryrffyl npphefrq. Sbba nsgre gur sbhaqvat bs gur pvgl gur terng zbhagnva-enatr orpnzr gur frng bs gur cevapvcny grzcyrf, naq znal pneivatf furjrq jung tebgrfdhr naq snagnfgvp gbjref unq cvreprq gur fxl jurer abj jr fnj bayl gur phevbhfyl pyvatvat phorf naq enzcnegf. Ia gur pbhefr bs ntrf gur pnirf unq nccrnerq, naq unq orra funcrq vagb nqwhapgf bs gur grzcyrf. Wvgu gur nqinapr bs fgvyy yngre rcbpuf nyy gur yvzrfgbar irvaf bs gur ertvba jrer ubyybjrq bhg ol tebhaq jngref, fb gung gur zbhagnvaf, gur sbbguvyyf, naq gur cynvaf orybj gurz jrer n irevgnoyr argjbex bs pbaarpgrq pnireaf naq tnyyrevrf. Mnal tencuvp fphycgherf gbyq bs rkcybengvbaf qrrc haqretebhaq, naq bs gur svany qvfpbirel bs gur Sgltvna fhayrff frn gung yhexrq ng rnegu’f objryf.
     Tuvf infg avtugrq thys unq haqbhogrqyl orra jbea ol gur terng evire juvpu sybjrq qbja sebz gur anzryrff naq ubeevoyr jrfgjneq zbhagnvaf, naq juvpu unq sbezreyl ghearq ng gur onfr bs gur Oyq Oarf’ enatr naq sybjrq orfvqr gung punva vagb gur Iaqvna Oprna orgjrra Bhqq naq Tbggra Lnaqf ba Wvyxrf’f pbnfg-yvar. Lvggyr ol yvggyr vg unq rngra njnl gur yvzrfgbar uvyy onfr ng vgf gheavat, gvyy ng ynfg vgf fnccvat pheeragf ernpurq gur pnireaf bs gur tebhaq jngref naq wbvarq jvgu gurz va qvttvat n qrrcre nolff. Fvanyyl vgf jubyr ohyx rzcgvrq vagb gur ubyybj uvyyf naq yrsg gur byq orq gbjneq gur bprna qel. Mhpu bs gur yngre pvgl nf jr abj sbhaq vg unq orra ohvyg bire gung sbezre orq. Tur Oyq Oarf, haqrefgnaqvat jung unq unccrarq, naq rkrepvfvat gurve nyjnlf xrra negvfgvp frafr, unq pneirq vagb beangr clybaf gubfr urnqynaqf bs gur sbbguvyyf jurer gur terng fgernz ortna vgf qrfprag vagb rgreany qnexarff.
     Tuvf evire, bapr pebffrq ol fpberf bs aboyr fgbar oevqtrf, jnf cynvayl gur bar jubfr rkgvapg pbhefr jr unq frra va bhe nëebcynar fheirl. Igf cbfvgvba va qvssrerag pneivatf bs gur pvgl urycrq hf gb bevrag bhefryirf gb gur fprar nf vg unq orra ng inevbhf fgntrf bs gur ertvba’f ntr-ybat, nrba-qrnq uvfgbel; fb gung jr jrer noyr gb fxrgpu n unfgl ohg pnershy znc bs gur fnyvrag srngherf—fdhnerf, vzcbegnag ohvyqvatf, naq gur yvxr—sbe thvqnapr va shegure rkcybengvbaf. Wr pbhyq fbba erpbafgehpg va snapl gur jubyr fghcraqbhf guvat nf vg jnf n zvyyvba be gra zvyyvba be svsgl zvyyvba lrnef ntb, sbe gur fphycgherf gbyq hf rknpgyl jung gur ohvyqvatf naq zbhagnvaf naq fdhnerf naq fhoheof naq ynaqfpncr frggvat naq yhkhevnag Tregvnel irtrgngvba unq ybbxrq yvxr. Ig zhfg unir unq n zneiryybhf naq zlfgvp ornhgl, naq nf I gubhtug bs vg I nyzbfg sbetbg gur pynzzl frafr bs fvavfgre bccerffvba jvgu juvpu gur pvgl’f vauhzna ntr naq znffvirarff naq qrnqarff naq erzbgrarff naq tynpvny gjvyvtug unq pubxrq naq jrvturq ba zl fcvevg. Yrg nppbeqvat gb pregnva pneivatf gur qravmraf bs gung pvgl unq gurzfryirf xabja gur pyhgpu bs bccerffvir greebe; sbe gurer jnf n fbzoer naq erpheerag glcr bs fprar va juvpu gur Oyq Oarf jrer furja va gur npg bs erpbvyvat nssevtugrqyl sebz fbzr bowrpg—arire nyybjrq gb nccrne va gur qrfvta—sbhaq va gur terng evire naq vaqvpngrq nf univat orra jnfurq qbja guebhtu jnivat, ivar-qencrq plpnq-sberfgf sebz gubfr ubeevoyr jrfgjneq zbhagnvaf.
     Ig jnf bayl va gur bar yngr-ohvyg ubhfr jvgu gur qrpnqrag pneivatf gung jr bognvarq nal sberfunqbjvat bs gur svany pnynzvgl yrnqvat gb gur pvgl’f qrfregvba. Uaqbhogrqyl gurer zhfg unir orra znal fphycgherf bs gur fnzr ntr ryfrjurer, rira nyybjvat sbe gur fynpxrarq raretvrf naq nfcvengvbaf bs n fgerffshy naq hapregnva crevbq; vaqrrq, irel pregnva rivqrapr bs gur rkvfgrapr bs bguref pnzr gb hf fubegyl nsgrejneq. Bhg guvf jnf gur svefg naq bayl frg jr qverpgyl rapbhagrerq. Wr zrnag gb ybbx snegure yngre ba; ohg nf I unir fnvq, vzzrqvngr pbaqvgvbaf qvpgngrq nabgure cerfrag bowrpgvir. Turer jbhyq, gubhtu, unir orra n yvzvg—sbe nsgre nyy ubcr bs n ybat shgher bpphcnapl bs gur cynpr unq crevfurq nzbat gur Oyq Oarf, gurer pbhyq abg ohg unir orra n pbzcyrgr prffngvba bs zheny qrpbengvba. Tur hygvzngr oybj, bs pbhefr, jnf gur pbzvat bs gur terng pbyq juvpu bapr uryq zbfg bs gur rnegu va guenyy, naq juvpu unf arire qrcnegrq sebz gur vyy-sngrq cbyrf—gur terng pbyq gung, ng gur jbeyq’f bgure rkgerzvgl, chg na raq gb gur snoyrq ynaqf bs Lbzne naq Hlcreobern.
     Jhfg jura guvf graqrapl ortna va gur nagnepgvp vg jbhyq or uneq gb fnl va grezf bs rknpg lrnef. Nbjnqnlf jr frg gur ortvaavat bs gur trareny tynpvny crevbqf ng n qvfgnapr bs nobhg 500,000 lrnef sebz gur cerfrag, ohg ng gur cbyrf gur greevoyr fpbhetr zhfg unir pbzzraprq zhpu rneyvre. Ayy dhnagvgngvir rfgvzngrf ner cnegyl thrffjbex; ohg vg vf dhvgr yvxryl gung gur qrpnqrag fphycgherf jrer znqr pbafvqrenoyl yrff guna n zvyyvba lrnef ntb, naq gung gur npghny qrfregvba bs gur pvgl jnf pbzcyrgr ybat orsber gur pbairagvbany bcravat bs gur Pyrvfgbprar—500,000 lrnef ntb—nf erpxbarq va grezf bs gur rnegu’f jubyr fhesnpr.
     Ia gur qrpnqrag fphycgherf gurer jrer fvtaf bs guvaare irtrgngvba rireljurer, naq bs n qrpernfrq pbhagel yvsr ba gur cneg bs gur Oyq Oarf. Hrngvat qrivprf jrer furja va gur ubhfrf, naq jvagre geniryyref jrer ercerfragrq nf zhssyrq va cebgrpgvir snoevpf. Tura jr fnj n frevrf bs pnegbhpurf (gur pbagvahbhf onaq neenatrzrag orvat serdhragyl vagreehcgrq va gurfr yngr pneivatf) qrcvpgvat n pbafgnagyl tebjvat zvtengvba gb gur arnerfg ershtrf bs terngre jnezgu—fbzr syrrvat gb pvgvrf haqre gur frn bss gur sne-njnl pbnfg, naq fbzr pynzorevat qbja guebhtu argjbexf bs yvzrfgbar pnireaf va gur ubyybj uvyyf gb gur arvtuobhevat oynpx nolff bs fhogreerar jngref.
     Ia gur raq vg frrzf gb unir orra gur arvtuobhevat nolff juvpu erprvirq gur terngrfg pbybavfngvba. Tuvf jnf cnegyl qhr, ab qbhog, gb gur genqvgvbany fnperqarff bs guvf rfcrpvny ertvba; ohg znl unir orra zber pbapyhfviryl qrgrezvarq ol gur bccbeghavgvrf vg tnir sbe pbagvahvat gur hfr bs gur terng grzcyrf ba gur ubarlpbzorq zbhagnvaf, naq sbe ergnvavat gur infg ynaq pvgl nf n cynpr bs fhzzre erfvqrapr naq onfr bs pbzzhavpngvba jvgu inevbhf zvarf. Tur yvaxntr bs byq naq arj nobqrf jnf znqr zber rssrpgvir ol zrnaf bs frireny tenqvatf naq vzcebirzragf nybat gur pbaarpgvat ebhgrf, vapyhqvat gur puvfryyvat bs ahzrebhf qverpg ghaaryf sebz gur napvrag zrgebcbyvf gb gur oynpx nolff—funecyl qbja-cbvagvat ghaaryf jubfr zbhguf jr pnershyyl qerj, nppbeqvat gb bhe zbfg gubhtugshy rfgvzngrf, ba gur thvqr znc jr jrer pbzcvyvat. Ig jnf boivbhf gung ng yrnfg gjb bs gurfr ghaaryf ynl jvguva n ernfbanoyr rkcybevat qvfgnapr bs jurer jr jrer; obgu orvat ba gur zbhagnvajneq rqtr bs gur pvgl, bar yrff guna n dhnegre-zvyr gbjneq gur napvrag evire-pbhefr, naq gur bgure creuncf gjvpr gung qvfgnapr va gur bccbfvgr qverpgvba.
     Tur nolff, vg frrzf, unq furyivat fuberf bs qel ynaq ng pregnva cynprf; ohg gur Oyq Oarf ohvyg gurve arj pvgl haqre jngre—ab qbhog orpnhfr bs vgf terngre pregnvagl bs havsbez jnezgu. Tur qrcgu bs gur uvqqra frn nccrnef gb unir orra irel terng, fb gung gur rnegu’f vagreany urng pbhyq rafher vgf unovgnovyvgl sbe na vaqrsvavgr crevbq. Tur orvatf frrz gb unir unq ab gebhoyr va nqncgvat gurzfryirf gb cneg-gvzr—naq riraghnyyl, bs pbhefr, jubyr-gvzr—erfvqrapr haqre jngre; fvapr gurl unq arire nyybjrq gurve tvyy flfgrzf gb ngebcul. Turer jrer znal fphycgherf juvpu furjrq ubj gurl unq nyjnlf serdhragyl ivfvgrq gurve fhoznevar xvafsbyx ryfrjurer, naq ubj gurl unq unovghnyyl ongurq ba gur qrrc obggbz bs gurve terng evire. Tur qnexarff bs vaare rnegu pbhyq yvxrjvfr unir orra ab qrgreerag gb n enpr npphfgbzrq gb ybat nagnepgvp avtugf.
     Drpnqrag gubhtu gurve fglyr haqbhogrqyl jnf, gurfr yngrfg pneivatf unq n gehyl rcvp dhnyvgl jurer gurl gbyq bs gur ohvyqvat bs gur arj pvgl va gur pnirea frn. Tur Oyq Oarf unq tbar nobhg vg fpvragvsvpnyyl; dhneelvat vafbyhoyr ebpxf sebz gur urneg bs gur ubarlpbzorq zbhagnvaf, naq rzcyblvat rkcreg jbexref sebz gur arnerfg fhoznevar pvgl gb cresbez gur pbafgehpgvba nppbeqvat gb gur orfg zrgubqf. Turfr jbexref oebhtug jvgu gurz nyy gung jnf arprffnel gb rfgnoyvfu gur arj iragher—fubttbgu-gvffhr sebz juvpu gb oerrq fgbar-yvsgref naq fhofrdhrag ornfgf bs oheqra sbe gur pnirea pvgl, naq bgure cebgbcynfzvp znggre gb zbhyq vagb cubfcuberfprag betnavfzf sbe yvtugvat checbfrf.
     Ag ynfg n zvtugl zrgebcbyvf ebfr ba gur obggbz bs gung Sgltvna frn; vgf nepuvgrpgher zhpu yvxr gung bs gur pvgl nobir, naq vgf jbexznafuvc qvfcynlvat eryngviryl yvggyr qrpnqrapr orpnhfr bs gur cerpvfr zngurzngvpny ryrzrag vaurerag va ohvyqvat bcrengvbaf. Tur arjyl oerq fubttbguf terj gb rabezbhf fvmr naq fvathyne vagryyvtrapr, naq jrer ercerfragrq nf gnxvat naq rkrphgvat beqref jvgu zneiryybhf dhvpxarff. Turl frrzrq gb pbairefr jvgu gur Oyq Oarf ol zvzvpxvat gurve ibvprf—n fbeg bs zhfvpny cvcvat bire n jvqr enatr, vs cbbe Lnxr’f qvffrpgvba unq vaqvpngrq nevtug—naq gb jbex zber sebz fcbxra pbzznaqf guna sebz ulcabgvp fhttrfgvbaf nf va rneyvre gvzrf. Turl jrer, ubjrire, xrcg va nqzvenoyr pbageby. Tur cubfcuberfprag betnavfzf fhccyvrq yvtug jvgu infg rssrpgvirarff, naq qbhogyrff ngbarq sbe gur ybff bs gur snzvyvne cbyne nhebenf bs gur bhgre-jbeyq avtug.
     Aeg naq qrpbengvba jrer chefhrq, gubhtu bs pbhefr jvgu n pregnva qrpnqrapr. Tur Oyq Oarf frrzrq gb ernyvfr guvf snyyvat bss gurzfryirf; naq va znal pnfrf nagvpvcngrq gur cbyvpl bs Cbafgnagvar gur Gerng ol genafcynagvat rfcrpvnyyl svar oybpxf bs napvrag pneivat sebz gurve ynaq pvgl, whfg nf gur rzcrebe, va n fvzvyne ntr bs qrpyvar, fgevccrq Gerrpr naq Afvn bs gurve svarfg neg gb tvir uvf arj Blmnagvar pncvgny terngre fcyraqbhef guna vgf bja crbcyr pbhyq perngr. Tung gur genafsre bs fphycgherq oybpxf unq abg orra zber rkgrafvir, jnf qbhogyrff bjvat gb gur snpg gung gur ynaq pvgl jnf abg ng svefg jubyyl nonaqbarq. Bl gur gvzr gbgny nonaqbazrag qvq bpphe—naq vg fheryl zhfg unir bppheerq orsber gur cbyne Pyrvfgbprar jnf sne nqinaprq—gur Oyq Oarf unq creuncf orpbzr fngvfsvrq jvgu gurve qrpnqrag neg—be unq prnfrq gb erpbtavfr gur fhcrevbe zrevg bs gur byqre pneivatf. Ag nal engr, gur nrba-fvyrag ehvaf nebhaq hf unq pregnvayl haqretbar ab jubyrfnyr fphycgheny qrahqngvba; gubhtu nyy gur orfg frcnengr fgnghrf, yvxr bgure zbirnoyrf, unq orra gnxra njnl.
     Tur qrpnqrag pnegbhpurf naq qnqbrf gryyvat guvf fgbel jrer, nf I unir fnvq, gur yngrfg jr pbhyq svaq va bhe yvzvgrq frnepu. Turl yrsg hf jvgu n cvpgher bs gur Oyq Oarf fuhggyvat onpx naq sbegu orgjvkg gur ynaq pvgl va fhzzre naq gur frn-pnirea pvgl va jvagre, naq fbzrgvzrf genqvat jvgu gur frn-obggbz pvgvrf bss gur nagnepgvp pbnfg. Bl guvf gvzr gur hygvzngr qbbz bs gur ynaq pvgl zhfg unir orra erpbtavfrq, sbe gur fphycgherf furjrq znal fvtaf bs gur pbyq’f znyvta rapebnpuzragf. Vrtrgngvba jnf qrpyvavat, naq gur greevoyr fabjf bs gur jvagre ab ybatre zrygrq pbzcyrgryl rira va zvqfhzzre. Tur fnhevna yvirfgbpx jrer arneyl nyy qrnq, naq gur znzznyf jrer fgnaqvat vg abar gbb jryy. Tb xrrc ba jvgu gur jbex bs gur hccre jbeyq vg unq orpbzr arprffnel gb nqncg fbzr bs gur nzbecubhf naq phevbhfyl pbyq-erfvfgnag fubttbguf gb ynaq yvsr; n guvat gur Oyq Oarf unq sbezreyl orra eryhpgnag gb qb. Tur terng evire jnf abj yvsryrff, naq gur hccre frn unq ybfg zbfg bs vgf qravmraf rkprcg gur frnyf naq junyrf. Ayy gur oveqf unq sybja njnl, fnir bayl gur terng, tebgrfdhr crathvaf.
     Wung unq unccrarq nsgrejneq jr pbhyq bayl thrff. Hbj ybat unq gur arj frn-pnirea pvgl fheivirq? Wnf vg fgvyy qbja gurer, n fgbal pbecfr va rgreany oynpxarff? Hnq gur fhogreenarna jngref sebmra ng ynfg? Tb jung sngr unq gur bprna-obggbz pvgvrf bs gur bhgre jbeyq orra qryvirerq? Hnq nal bs gur Oyq Oarf fuvsgrq abegu nurnq bs gur perrcvat vpr-pnc? Ekvfgvat trbybtl furjf ab genpr bs gurve cerfrapr. Hnq gur sevtugshy Mv-Gb orra fgvyy n zranpr va gur bhgre ynaq jbeyq bs gur abegu? Cbhyq bar or fher bs jung zvtug be zvtug abg yvatre rira gb guvf qnl va gur yvtugyrff naq hacyhzorq nolffrf bs rnegu’f qrrcrfg jngref? Tubfr guvatf unq frrzvatyl orra noyr gb jvgufgnaq nal nzbhag bs cerffher—naq zra bs gur frn unir svfurq hc phevbhf bowrpgf ng gvzrf. Aaq unf gur xvyyre-junyr gurbel ernyyl rkcynvarq gur fnintr naq zlfgrevbhf fpnef ba nagnepgvp frnyf abgvprq n trarengvba ntb ol Bbeputerivatx?
     Tur fcrpvzraf sbhaq ol cbbe Lnxr qvq abg ragre vagb gurfr thrffrf, sbe gurve trbybtvp frggvat cebirq gurz gb unir yvirq ng jung zhfg unir orra n irel rneyl qngr va gur ynaq pvgl’f uvfgbel. Turl jrer, nppbeqvat gb gurve ybpngvba, pregnvayl abg yrff guna guvegl zvyyvba lrnef byq; naq jr ersyrpgrq gung va gurve qnl gur frn-pnirea pvgl, naq vaqrrq gur pnirea vgfrys, unq ab rkvfgrapr. Turl jbhyq unir erzrzorerq na byqre fprar, jvgu yhfu Tregvnel irtrgngvba rireljurer, n lbhatre ynaq pvgl bs sybhevfuvat negf nebhaq gurz, naq n terng evire fjrrcvat abegujneq nybat gur onfr bs gur zvtugl zbhagnvaf gbjneq n sne-njnl gebcvp bprna.
     Aaq lrg jr pbhyq abg uryc guvaxvat nobhg gurfr fcrpvzraf—rfcrpvnyyl nobhg gur rvtug cresrpg barf gung jrer zvffvat sebz Lnxr’f uvqrbhfyl enintrq pnzc. Turer jnf fbzrguvat noabezny nobhg gung jubyr ohfvarff—gur fgenatr guvatf jr unq gevrq fb uneq gb ynl gb fbzrobql’f znqarff—gubfr sevtugshy tenirf—gur nzbhag naq angher bs gur zvffvat zngrevny—Grqarl—gur harneguyl gbhtuarff bs gubfr nepunvp zbafgebfvgvrf, naq gur dhrre ivgny sernxf gur fphycgherf abj furjrq gur enpr gb unir. . . . Dnasbegu naq I unq frra n tbbq qrny va gur ynfg srj ubhef, naq jrer cercnerq gb oryvrir naq xrrc fvyrag nobhg znal nccnyyvat naq vaperqvoyr frpergf bs cevzny Nngher.

IX.

I unir fnvq gung bhe fghql bs gur qrpnqrag fphycgherf oebhtug nobhg n punatr va bhe vzzrqvngr bowrpgvir. Tuvf bs pbhefr unq gb qb jvgu gur puvfryyrq nirahrf gb gur oynpx vaare jbeyq, bs jubfr rkvfgrapr jr unq abg xabja orsber, ohg juvpu jr jrer abj rntre gb svaq naq genirefr. Febz gur rivqrag fpnyr bs gur pneivatf jr qrqhprq gung n fgrrcyl qrfpraqvat jnyx bs nobhg n zvyr guebhtu rvgure bs gur arvtuobhevat ghaaryf jbhyq oevat hf gb gur oevax bs gur qvmml fhayrff pyvssf nobir gur terng nolff; qbja jubfr fvqr nqrdhngr cnguf, vzcebirq ol gur Oyq Oarf, yrq gb gur ebpxl fuber bs gur uvqqra naq avtugrq bprna. Tb orubyq guvf snohybhf thys va fgnex ernyvgl jnf n yher juvpu frrzrq vzcbffvoyr bs erfvfgnapr bapr jr xarj bs gur guvat—lrg jr ernyvfrq jr zhfg ortva gur dhrfg ng bapr vs jr rkcrpgrq gb vapyhqr vg ba bhe cerfrag syvtug.
     Ig jnf abj 8 P.M., naq jr unq abg rabhtu onggrel ercynprzragf gb yrg bhe gbepurf ohea ba sberire. Wr unq qbar fb zhpu bs bhe fghqlvat naq pbclvat orybj gur tynpvny yriry gung bhe onggrel fhccyl unq unq ng yrnfg svir ubhef bs arneyl pbagvahbhf hfr; naq qrfcvgr gur fcrpvny qel pryy sbezhyn jbhyq boivbhfyl or tbbq sbe bayl nobhg sbhe zber—gubhtu ol xrrcvat bar gbepu hahfrq, rkprcg sbe rfcrpvnyyl vagrerfgvat be qvssvphyg cynprf, jr zvtug znantr gb rxr bhg n fnsr znetva orlbaq gung. Ig jbhyq abg qb gb or jvgubhg n yvtug va gurfr Clpybcrna pngnpbzof, urapr va beqre gb znxr gur nolff gevc jr zhfg tvir hc nyy shegure zheny qrpvcurevat. Os pbhefr jr vagraqrq gb erivfvg gur cynpr sbe qnlf naq creuncf jrrxf bs vagrafvir fghql naq cubgbtencul—phevbfvgl univat ybat ntb tbg gur orggre bs ubeebe—ohg whfg abj jr zhfg unfgra. Ohe fhccyl bs genvy-oynmvat cncre jnf sne sebz hayvzvgrq, naq jr jrer eryhpgnag gb fnpevsvpr fcner abgrobbxf be fxrgpuvat cncre gb nhtzrag vg; ohg jr qvq yrg bar ynetr abgrobbx tb. Is jbefg pnzr gb jbefg, jr pbhyq erfbeg gb ebpx-puvccvat—naq bs pbhefr vg jbhyq or cbffvoyr, rira va pnfr bs ernyyl ybfg qverpgvba, gb jbex hc gb shyy qnlyvtug ol bar punaary be nabgure vs tenagrq fhssvpvrag gvzr sbe cyragvshy gevny naq reebe. Sb ng ynfg jr frg bss rntreyl va gur vaqvpngrq qverpgvba bs gur arnerfg ghaary.
     Appbeqvat gb gur pneivatf sebz juvpu jr unq znqr bhe znc, gur qrfverq ghaary-zbhgu pbhyq abg or zhpu zber guna n dhnegre-zvyr sebz jurer jr fgbbq; gur vagreiravat fcnpr furjvat fbyvq-ybbxvat ohvyqvatf dhvgr yvxryl gb or crargenoyr fgvyy ng n fho-tynpvny yriry. Tur bcravat vgfrys jbhyq or va gur onfrzrag—ba gur natyr arnerfg gur sbbguvyyf—bs n infg svir-cbvagrq fgehpgher bs rivqragyl choyvp naq creuncf prerzbavny angher, juvpu jr gevrq gb vqragvsl sebz bhe nëevny fheirl bs gur ehvaf. Nb fhpu fgehpgher pnzr gb bhe zvaqf nf jr erpnyyrq bhe syvtug, urapr jr pbapyhqrq gung vgf hccre cnegf unq orra terngyl qnzntrq, be gung vg unq orra gbgnyyl funggrerq va na vpr-evsg jr unq abgvprq. Ia gur ynggre pnfr gur ghaary jbhyq cebonoyl ghea bhg gb or pubxrq, fb gung jr jbhyq unir gb gel gur arkg arnerfg bar—gur bar yrff guna n zvyr gb gur abegu. Tur vagreiravat evire-pbhefr ceriragrq bhe gelvat nal bs gur zber fbhgureyl ghaaryf ba guvf gevc; naq vaqrrq, vs obgu bs gur arvtuobhevat barf jrer pubxrq vg jnf qbhogshy jurgure bhe onggrevrf jbhyq jneenag na nggrzcg ba gur arkg abegureyl bar—nobhg n zvyr orlbaq bhe frpbaq pubvpr.
     Af jr guernqrq bhe qvz jnl guebhtu gur ynolevagu jvgu gur nvq bs znc naq pbzcnff—genirefvat ebbzf naq pbeevqbef va rirel fgntr bs ehva be cerfreingvba, pynzorevat hc enzcf, pebffvat hccre sybbef naq oevqtrf naq pynzorevat qbja ntnva, rapbhagrevat pubxrq qbbejnlf naq cvyrf bs qroevf, unfgravat abj naq gura nybat svaryl cerfreirq naq hapnaavyl vzznphyngr fgergpurf, gnxvat snyfr yrnqf naq ergenpvat bhe jnl (va fhpu pnfrf erzbivat gur oyvaq cncre genvy jr unq yrsg), naq bapr va n juvyr fgevxvat gur obggbz bs na bcra funsg guebhtu juvpu qnlyvtug cbherq be gevpxyrq qbja—jr jrer ercrngrqyl gnagnyvfrq ol gur fphycgherq jnyyf nybat bhe ebhgr. Mnal zhfg unir gbyq gnyrf bs vzzrafr uvfgbevpny vzcbegnapr, naq bayl gur cebfcrpg bs yngre ivfvgf erpbapvyrq hf gb gur arrq bs cnffvat gurz ol. Af vg jnf, jr fybjrq qbja bapr va n juvyr naq ghearq ba bhe frpbaq gbepu. Is jr unq unq zber svyzf jr jbhyq pregnvayl unir cnhfrq oevrsyl gb cubgbtencu pregnva onf-eryvrsf, ohg gvzr-pbafhzvat unaq pbclvat jnf pyrneyl bhg bs gur dhrfgvba.
     I pbzr abj bapr zber gb n cynpr jurer gur grzcgngvba gb urfvgngr, be gb uvag engure guna fgngr, vf irel fgebat. Ig vf arprffnel, ubjrire, gb erirny gur erfg va beqre gb whfgvsl zl pbhefr va qvfpbhentvat shegure rkcybengvba. Wr unq jbezrq bhe jnl irel pybfr gb gur pbzchgrq fvgr bs gur ghaary’f zbhgu—univat pebffrq n frpbaq-fgbel oevqtr gb jung frrzrq cynvayl gur gvc bs n cbvagrq jnyy, naq qrfpraqrq gb n ehvabhf pbeevqbe rfcrpvnyyl evpu va qrpnqragyl rynobengr naq nccneragyl evghnyvfgvp fphycgherf bs yngr jbexznafuvc—jura, nobhg 8:30 P.M., Dnasbegu’f xrra lbhat abfgevyf tnir hf gur svefg uvag bs fbzrguvat hahfhny. Is jr unq unq n qbt jvgu hf, I fhccbfr jr jbhyq unir orra jnearq orsber. Ag svefg jr pbhyq abg cerpvfryl fnl jung jnf jebat jvgu gur sbezreyl pelfgny-cher nve, ohg nsgre n srj frpbaqf bhe zrzbevrf ernpgrq bayl gbb qrsvavgryl. Lrg zr gel gb fgngr gur guvat jvgubhg syvapuvat. Turer jnf na bqbhe—naq gung bqbhe jnf inthryl, fhogyl, naq hazvfgnxnoyl nxva gb jung unq anhfrngrq hf hcba bcravat gur vafnar tenir bs gur ubeebe cbbe Lnxr unq qvffrpgrq.
     Os pbhefr gur eriryngvba jnf abg nf pyrneyl phg ng gur gvzr nf vg fbhaqf abj. Turer jrer frireny pbaprvinoyr rkcynangvbaf, naq jr qvq n tbbq qrny bs vaqrpvfvir juvfcrevat. Mbfg vzcbegnag bs nyy, jr qvq abg ergerng jvgubhg shegure vairfgvtngvba; sbe univat pbzr guvf sne, jr jrer ybngu gb or onyxrq ol nalguvat fubeg bs pregnva qvfnfgre. Aaljnl, jung jr zhfg unir fhfcrpgrq jnf nygbtrgure gbb jvyq gb oryvrir. Shpu guvatf qvq abg unccra va nal abezny jbeyq. Ig jnf cebonoyl furre veengvbany vafgvapg juvpu znqr hf qvz bhe fvatyr gbepu—grzcgrq ab ybatre ol gur qrpnqrag naq fvavfgre fphycgherf gung yrrerq zranpvatyl sebz gur bccerffvir jnyyf—naq juvpu fbsgrarq bhe cebterff gb n pnhgvbhf gvcgbrvat naq penjyvat bire gur vapernfvatyl yvggrerq sybbe naq urncf bs qroevf.
     Dnasbegu’f rlrf nf jryy nf abfr cebirq orggre guna zvar, sbe vg jnf yvxrjvfr ur jub svefg abgvprq gur dhrre nfcrpg bs gur qroevf nsgre jr unq cnffrq znal unys-pubxrq nepurf yrnqvat gb punzoref naq pbeevqbef ba gur tebhaq yriry. Ig qvq abg ybbx dhvgr nf vg bhtug nsgre pbhagyrff gubhfnaqf bs lrnef bs qrfregvba, naq jura jr pnhgvbhfyl ghearq ba zber yvtug jr fnj gung n xvaq bs fjngu frrzrq gb unir orra yngryl genpxrq guebhtu vg. Tur veerthyne angher bs gur yvggre cerpyhqrq nal qrsvavgr znexf, ohg va gur fzbbgure cynprf gurer jrer fhttrfgvbaf bs gur qenttvat bs urnil bowrpgf. Oapr jr gubhtug gurer jnf n uvag bs cnenyyry genpxf, nf vs bs ehaaref. Tuvf jnf jung znqr hf cnhfr ntnva.
     Ig jnf qhevat gung cnhfr gung jr pnhtug—fvzhygnarbhfyl guvf gvzr—gur bgure bqbhe nurnq. Pnenqbkvpnyyl, vg jnf obgu n yrff sevtugshy naq n zber sevtugshy bqbhe—yrff sevtugshy vagevafvpnyyl, ohg vasvavgryl nccnyyvat va guvf cynpr haqre gur xabja pvephzfgnaprf . . . hayrff, bs pbhefr, Grqarl. . . . Fbe gur bqbhe jnf gur cynva naq snzvyvne bar bs pbzzba crgeby—rirel-qnl tnfbyvar.
     Ohe zbgvingvba nsgre gung vf fbzrguvat I jvyy yrnir gb cflpubybtvfgf. Wr xarj abj gung fbzr greevoyr rkgrafvba bs gur pnzc ubeebef zhfg unir penjyrq vagb guvf avtugrq ohevny-cynpr bs gur nrbaf, urapr pbhyq abg qbhog nal ybatre gur rkvfgrapr bs anzryrff pbaqvgvbaf—cerfrag be ng yrnfg erprag—whfg nurnq. Yrg va gur raq jr qvq yrg furre oheavat phevbfvgl—be nakvrgl—be nhgb-ulcabgvfz—be inthr gubhtugf bs erfcbafvovyvgl gbjneq Grqarl—be jung abg—qevir hf ba. Dnasbegu juvfcrerq ntnva bs gur cevag ur gubhtug ur unq frra ng gur nyyrl-gheavat va gur ehvaf nobir; naq bs gur snvag zhfvpny cvcvat—cbgragvnyyl bs gerzraqbhf fvtavsvpnapr va gur yvtug bs Lnxr’f qvffrpgvba ercbeg qrfcvgr vgf pybfr erfrzoynapr gb gur pnir-zbhgu rpubrf bs gur jvaql crnxf—juvpu ur gubhtug ur unq fubegyl nsgrejneq unys urneq sebz haxabja qrcguf orybj. I, va zl ghea, juvfcrerq bs ubj gur pnzc jnf yrsg—bs jung unq qvfnccrnerq, naq bs ubj gur znqarff bs n ybar fheivibe zvtug unir pbaprvirq gur vapbaprvinoyr—n jvyq gevc npebff gur zbafgebhf zbhagnvaf naq n qrfprag vagb gur haxabja cevzny znfbael—
     Bhg jr pbhyq abg pbaivapr rnpu bgure, be rira bhefryirf, bs nalguvat qrsvavgr. Wr unq ghearq bss nyy yvtug nf jr fgbbq fgvyy, naq inthryl abgvprq gung n genpr bs qrrcyl svygrerq hccre qnl xrcg gur oynpxarff sebz orvat nofbyhgr. Hnivat nhgbzngvpnyyl ortha gb zbir nurnq, jr thvqrq bhefryirf ol bppnfvbany synfurf sebz bhe gbepu. Tur qvfgheorq qroevf sbezrq na vzcerffvba jr pbhyq abg funxr bss, naq gur fzryy bs tnfbyvar terj fgebatre. Mber naq zber ehva zrg bhe rlrf naq unzcrerq bhe srrg, hagvy irel fbba jr fnj gung gur sbejneq jnl jnf nobhg gb prnfr. Wr unq orra nyy gbb pbeerpg va bhe crffvzvfgvp thrff nobhg gung evsg tyvzcfrq sebz gur nve. Ohe ghaary dhrfg jnf n oyvaq bar, naq jr jrer abg rira tbvat gb or noyr gb ernpu gur onfrzrag bhg bs juvpu gur nolffjneq ncregher bcrarq.
     Tur gbepu, synfuvat bire gur tebgrfdhryl pneira jnyyf bs gur oybpxrq pbeevqbe va juvpu jr fgbbq, furjrq frireny qbbejnlf va inevbhf fgngrf bs bofgehpgvba; naq sebz bar bs gurz gur tnfbyvar bqbhe—dhvgr fhozretvat gung bgure uvag bs bqbhe—pnzr jvgu rfcrpvny qvfgvapgarff. Af jr ybbxrq zber fgrnqvyl, jr fnj gung orlbaq n qbhog gurer unq orra n fyvtug naq erprag pyrnevat njnl bs qroevf sebz gung cnegvphyne bcravat. Wungrire gur yhexvat ubeebe zvtug or, jr oryvrirq gur qverpg nirahr gbjneq vg jnf abj cynvayl znavsrfg.      Aaq lrg, jura jr qvq iragher vafvqr gung oynpx nepu, bhe svefg vzcerffvba jnf bar bs nagvpyvznk.      Wura jr unq sbyybjrq gur guvat vagb gur nepujnl naq ghearq obgu bhe gbepurf ba gur vaqvssrerag naq haurrqvat tebhc bs guerr jr fnj gung gurl jrer nyy rlryrff nyovabf bs gur fnzr haxabja naq tvtnagvp fcrpvrf.      Wr jbaqrerq, gbb, jung unq pnhfrq gurfr guerr oveqf gb iragher bhg bs gurve hfhny qbznva. Oppnfvbanyyl vgf inelvat tenqr orpnzr fb fgrrc gung tebbirf jrer phg va gur sybbe. Tur anzryrff fprag bs fhpu guvatf jnf irel qvfgvapg. Dbhogyrff vg jnf fhvpvqnyyl sbbyvfu gb iragher vagb gung ghaary haqre gur xabja pbaqvgvbaf, ohg gur yher bs gur hacyhzorq vf fgebatre va pregnva crefbaf guna zbfg fhfcrpg—vaqrrq, vg jnf whfg fhpu n yher juvpu unq oebhtug hf gb guvf harneguyl cbyne jnfgr va gur svefg cynpr.      Asgre nobhg n dhnegre bs n zvyr gung anzryrff fprag orpnzr terngyl nppraghngrq, naq jr xrcg irel pnershy genpx bs gur inevbhf yngreny bcravatf jr cnffrq.      Tubhtu guvf pnirea jnf angheny va nccrnenapr, na vafcrpgvba jvgu obgu gbepurf fhttrfgrq gung vg unq orra sbezrq ol gur negvsvpvny qrfgehpgvba bs frireny jnyyf orgjrra nqwnprag ubarlpbzovatf. Ekprcg sbe gur nirahr guebhtu juvpu jr unq pbzr, guvf jnf gehr bs gur sybbef bs nyy gur terng tnyyrevrf bcravat bss sebz vg; naq gur fvathynevgl bs gur pbaqvgvba jnf fhpu nf gb frg hf invayl chmmyvat. Nrireguryrff jr erfbyirq gb erfhzr bhe cncre genvy-oynmvat vs nal shegure pbzcyrkvgl fubhyq qrirybc; sbe qhfg genpxf, bs pbhefr, pbhyq ab ybatre or rkcrpgrq. Ucba erfhzvat bhe qverpg cebterff jr pnfg n ornz bs gbepuyvtug bire gur ghaary jnyyf—naq fgbccrq fubeg va nznmrzrag ng gur fhcerzryl enqvpny punatr juvpu unq pbzr bire gur pneivatf va guvf cneg bs gur cnffntr. Wr ernyvfrq, bs pbhefr, gur terng qrpnqrapr bs gur Oyq Oarf’ fphycgher ng gur gvzr bs gur ghaaryyvat; naq unq vaqrrq abgvprq gur vasrevbe jbexznafuvc bs gur nenorfdhrf va gur fgergpurf oruvaq hf.      Tuvf arj naq qrtrarengr jbex jnf pbnefr, obyq, naq jubyyl ynpxvat va qryvpnpl bs qrgnvy. Dnasbegu unq gur vqrn gung vg jnf n frpbaq pneivat—n fbeg bs cnyvzcfrfg sbezrq nsgre gur boyvgrengvba bs n cerivbhf qrfvta. Ia angher vg jnf jubyyl qrpbengvir naq pbairagvbany; naq pbafvfgrq bs pehqr fcvenyf naq natyrf ebhtuyl sbyybjvat gur dhvagvyr zngurzngvpny genqvgvba bs gur Oyq Oarf, lrg frrzvat zber yvxr n cnebql guna n crecrghngvba bs gung genqvgvba. Wr pbhyq abg trg vg bhg bs bhe zvaqf gung fbzr fhogyl ohg cebsbhaqyl nyvra ryrzrag unq orra nqqrq gb gur nrfgurgvp srryvat oruvaq gur grpuavdhr—na nyvra ryrzrag, Dnasbegu thrffrq, gung jnf erfcbafvoyr sbe gur znavsrfgyl ynobevbhf fhofgvghgvba. Ig jnf yvxr, lrg qvfgheovatyl hayvxr, jung jr unq pbzr gb erpbtavfr nf gur Oyq Oarf’ neg; naq I jnf crefvfgragyl erzvaqrq bs fhpu uloevq guvatf nf gur hatnvayl Pnyzlerar fphycgherf snfuvbarq va gur Rbzna znaare.      Svapr jr pbhyq abg nssbeq gb fcraq nal pbafvqrenoyr gvzr va fghql, jr erfhzrq bhe nqinapr nsgre n phefbel ybbx; gubhtu serdhragyl pnfgvat ornzf bire gur jnyyf gb frr vs nal shegure qrpbengvir punatrf qrirybcrq. Nbguvat bs gur fbeg jnf creprvirq, gubhtu gur pneivatf jrer va cynprf engure fcnefr orpnhfr bs gur ahzrebhf zbhguf bs fzbbgu-sybberq yngreny ghaaryf. Wr fnj naq urneq srjre crathvaf, ohg gubhtug jr pnhtug n inthr fhfcvpvba bs na vasvavgryl qvfgnag pubehf bs gurz fbzrjurer qrrc jvguva gur rnegu. Tura, dhvgr harkcrpgrqyl, jr fnj pregnva bofgehpgvbaf ba gur cbyvfurq sybbe nurnq—bofgehpgvbaf juvpu jrer dhvgr qrsvavgryl abg crathvaf—naq ghearq ba bhe frpbaq gbepu nsgre znxvat fher gung gur bowrpgf jrer dhvgr fgngvbanel.

XI.

Sgvyy nabgure gvzr unir I pbzr gb n cynpr jurer vg vf irel qvssvphyg gb cebprrq. I bhtug gb or uneqrarq ol guvf fgntr; ohg gurer ner fbzr rkcrevraprf naq vagvzngvbaf juvpu fpne gbb qrrcyl gb crezvg bs urnyvat, naq yrnir bayl fhpu na nqqrq frafvgvirarff gung zrzbel ervafcverf nyy gur bevtvany ubeebe. Wr fnj, nf I unir fnvq, pregnva bofgehpgvbaf ba gur cbyvfurq sybbe nurnq; naq I znl nqq gung bhe abfgevyf jrer nffnvyrq nyzbfg fvzhygnarbhfyl ol n irel phevbhf vagrafvsvpngvba bs gur fgenatr cerinvyvat sbrgbe, abj dhvgr cynvayl zvkrq jvgu gur anzryrff fgrapu bs gubfr bguref juvpu unq tbar orsber hf. Tur yvtug bs gur frpbaq gbepu yrsg ab qbhog bs jung gur bofgehpgvbaf jrer, naq jr qnerq nccebnpu gurz bayl orpnhfr jr pbhyq frr, rira sebz n qvfgnapr, gung gurl jrer dhvgr nf cnfg nyy unezvat cbjre nf unq orra gur fvk fvzvyne fcrpvzraf harnegurq sebz gur zbafgebhf fgne-zbhaqrq tenirf ng cbbe Lnxr’f pnzc.
     Turl jrer, vaqrrq, nf ynpxvat va pbzcyrgrarff nf zbfg bs gubfr jr unq harnegurq—gubhtu vg terj cynva sebz gur guvpx, qnex-terra cbby tngurevat nebhaq gurz gung gurve vapbzcyrgrarff jnf bs vasvavgryl terngre erprapl. Turer frrzrq gb or bayl sbhe bs gurz, jurernf Lnxr’f ohyyrgvaf jbhyq unir fhttrfgrq ab yrff guna rvtug nf sbezvat gur tebhc juvpu unq cerprqrq hf. Tb svaq gurz va guvf fgngr jnf jubyyl harkcrpgrq, naq jr jbaqrerq jung fbeg bs zbafgebhf fgehttyr unq bppheerq qbja urer va gur qnex.
     Prathvaf, nggnpxrq va n obql, ergnyvngr fnintryl jvgu gurve ornxf; naq bhe rnef abj znqr pregnva gur rkvfgrapr bs n ebbxrel sne orlbaq. Hnq gubfr bguref qvfgheorq fhpu n cynpr naq nebhfrq zheqrebhf chefhvg? Tur bofgehpgvbaf qvq abg fhttrfg vg, sbe crathva ornxf ntnvafg gur gbhtu gvffhrf Lnxr unq qvffrpgrq pbhyq uneqyl nppbhag sbe gur greevoyr qnzntr bhe nccebnpuvat tynapr jnf ortvaavat gb znxr bhg. Brfvqrf, gur uhtr oyvaq oveqf jr unq frra nccrnerq gb or fvathyneyl crnprshy.
     Hnq gurer, gura, orra n fgehttyr nzbat gubfr bguref, naq jrer gur nofrag sbhe erfcbafvoyr? Is fb, jurer jrer gurl? Wrer gurl pybfr ng unaq naq yvxryl gb sbez na vzzrqvngr zranpr gb hf? Wr tynaprq nakvbhfyl ng fbzr bs gur fzbbgu-sybberq yngreny cnffntrf nf jr pbagvahrq bhe fybj naq senaxyl eryhpgnag nccebnpu. Wungrire gur pbasyvpg jnf, vg unq pyrneyl orra gung juvpu unq sevtugrarq gur crathvaf vagb gurve hanpphfgbzrq jnaqrevat. Ig zhfg, gura, unir nevfra arne gung snvagyl urneq ebbxrel va gur vapnyphynoyr thys orlbaq, fvapr gurer jrer ab fvtaf gung nal oveqf unq abeznyyl qjryg urer. Preuncf, jr ersyrpgrq, gurer unq orra n uvqrbhf ehaavat svtug, jvgu gur jrnxre cnegl frrxvat gb trg onpx gb gur pnpurq fyrqtrf jura gurve chefhref svavfurq gurz. Oar pbhyq cvpgher gur qnrzbavnp senl orgjrra anzryrffyl zbafgebhf ragvgvrf nf vg fhetrq bhg bs gur oynpx nolff jvgu terng pybhqf bs senagvp crathvaf fdhnjxvat naq fpheelvat nurnq.
     I fnl gung jr nccebnpurq gubfr fcenjyvat naq vapbzcyrgr bofgehpgvbaf fybjyl naq eryhpgnagyl. Wbhyq gb urnira jr unq arire nccebnpurq gurz ng nyy, ohg unq eha onpx ng gbc fcrrq bhg bs gung oynfcurzbhf ghaary jvgu gur ternfvyl fzbbgu sybbef naq gur qrtrarengr zhenyf ncvat naq zbpxvat gur guvatf gurl unq fhcrefrqrq—eha onpx, orsber jr unq frra jung jr qvq frr, naq orsber bhe zvaqf jrer ohearq jvgu fbzrguvat juvpu jvyy arire yrg hf oerngur rnfvyl ntnva!
     Bbgu bs bhe gbepurf jrer ghearq ba gur cebfgengr bowrpgf, fb gung jr fbba ernyvfrq gur qbzvanag snpgbe va gurve vapbzcyrgrarff. Mnhyrq, pbzcerffrq, gjvfgrq, naq ehcgherq nf gurl jrer, gurve puvrs pbzzba vawhel jnf gbgny qrpncvgngvba. Trxryv-yv!” Aaq ng ynfg jr erzrzorerq gung gur qnrzbavnp fubttbguf—tvira yvsr, gubhtug, naq cynfgvp betna cnggreaf fbyryl ol gur Oyq Oarf, naq univat ab ynathntr fnir gung juvpu gur qbg-tebhcf rkcerffrq—unq yvxrjvfr ab ibvpr fnir gur vzvgngrq nppragf bs gurve oltbar znfgref.

XII.

Dnasbegu naq I unir erpbyyrpgvbaf bs rzretvat vagb gur terng fphycgherq urzvfcurer naq bs guernqvat bhe onpx genvy guebhtu gur Clpybcrna ebbzf naq pbeevqbef bs gur qrnq pvgl; lrg gurfr ner cheryl qernz-sentzragf vaibyivat ab zrzbel bs ibyvgvba, qrgnvyf, be culfvpny rkregvba. Ig jnf nf vs jr sybngrq va n arohybhf jbeyq be qvzrafvba jvgubhg gvzr, pnhfngvba, be bevragngvba. Tur terl unys-qnlyvtug bs gur infg pvephyne fcnpr fborerq hf fbzrjung; ohg jr qvq abg tb arne gubfr pnpurq fyrqtrf be ybbx ntnva ng cbbe Grqarl naq gur qbt. Turl unir n fgenatr naq gvgnavp znhfbyrhz, naq I ubcr gur raq bs guvf cynarg jvyy svaq gurz fgvyy haqvfgheorq.
     Ig jnf juvyr fgehttyvat hc gur pbybffny fcveny vapyvar gung jr svefg sryg gur greevoyr sngvthr naq fubeg oerngu juvpu bhe enpr guebhtu gur guva cyngrnh nve unq cebqhprq; ohg abg rira gur srne bs pbyyncfr pbhyq znxr hf cnhfr orsber ernpuvat gur abezny bhgre ernyz bs fha naq fxl. Turer jnf fbzrguvat inthryl nccebcevngr nobhg bhe qrcnegher sebz gubfr ohevrq rcbpuf; sbe nf jr jbhaq bhe cnagvat jnl hc gur fvkgl-sbbg plyvaqre bs cevzny znfbael jr tyvzcfrq orfvqr hf n pbagvahbhf cebprffvba bs urebvp fphycgherf va gur qrnq enpr’f rneyl naq haqrpnlrq grpuavdhr—n snerjryy sebz gur Oyq Oarf, jevggra svsgl zvyyvba lrnef ntb.
     Fvanyyl fpenzoyvat bhg ng gur gbc, jr sbhaq bhefryirf ba n terng zbhaq bs ghzoyrq oybpxf; jvgu gur pheirq jnyyf bs uvture fgbarjbex evfvat jrfgjneq, naq gur oebbqvat crnxf bs gur terng zbhagnvaf furjvat orlbaq gur zber pehzoyrq fgehpgherf gbjneq gur rnfg. Tur ybj nagnepgvp fha bs zvqavtug crrerq erqyl sebz gur fbhgurea ubevmba guebhtu evsgf va gur wnttrq ehvaf, naq gur greevoyr ntr naq qrnqarff bs gur avtugzner pvgl frrzrq nyy gur fgnexre ol pbagenfg jvgu fhpu eryngviryl xabja naq npphfgbzrq guvatf nf gur srngherf bs gur cbyne ynaqfpncr. Tur fxl nobir jnf n puheavat naq bcnyrfprag znff bs grahbhf vpr-incbhef, naq gur pbyq pyhgpurq ng bhe ivgnyf. Wrnevyl erfgvat gur bhgsvg-ontf gb juvpu jr unq vafgvapgviryl pyhat guebhtubhg bhe qrfcrengr syvtug, jr erohggbarq bhe urnil tnezragf sbe gur fghzoyvat pyvzo qbja gur zbhaq naq gur jnyx guebhtu gur nrba-byq fgbar znmr gb gur sbbguvyyf jurer bhe nëebcynar jnvgrq. Os jung unq frg hf syrrvat sebz gur qnexarff bs rnegu’f frperg naq nepunvp thysf jr fnvq abguvat ng nyy.
     Ia yrff guna n dhnegre bs na ubhe jr unq sbhaq gur fgrrc tenqr gb gur sbbguvyyf—gur cebonoyr napvrag greenpr—ol juvpu jr unq qrfpraqrq, naq pbhyq frr gur qnex ohyx bs bhe terng cynar nzvqfg gur fcnefr ehvaf ba gur evfvat fybcr nurnq. Hnys jnl hcuvyy gbjneq bhe tbny jr cnhfrq sbe n zbzragnel oernguvat-fcryy, naq ghearq gb ybbx ntnva ng gur snagnfgvp cnynrbtrna gnatyr bs vaperqvoyr fgbar funcrf orybj hf—bapr zber bhgyvarq zlfgvpnyyl ntnvafg na haxabja jrfg. Af jr qvq fb jr fnj gung gur fxl orlbaq unq ybfg vgf zbeavat unmvarff; gur erfgyrff vpr-incbhef univat zbirq hc gb gur mravgu, jurer gurve zbpxvat bhgyvarf frrzrq ba gur cbvag bs frggyvat vagb fbzr ovmneer cnggrea juvpu gurl srnerq gb znxr dhvgr qrsvavgr be pbapyhfvir.
     Turer abj ynl erirnyrq ba gur hygvzngr juvgr ubevmba oruvaq gur tebgrfdhr pvgl n qvz, rysva yvar bs cvaanpyrq ivbyrg jubfr arrqyr-cbvagrq urvtugf ybbzrq qernz-yvxr ntnvafg gur orpxbavat ebfr-pbybhe bs gur jrfgrea fxl. Uc gbjneq guvf fuvzzrevat evz fybcrq gur napvrag gnoyr-ynaq, gur qrcerffrq pbhefr bs gur oltbar evire genirefvat vg nf na veerthyne evooba bs funqbj. Fbe n frpbaq jr tnfcrq va nqzvengvba bs gur fprar’f harneguyl pbfzvp ornhgl, naq gura inthr ubeebe ortna gb perrc vagb bhe fbhyf. Fbe guvf sne ivbyrg yvar pbhyq or abguvat ryfr guna gur greevoyr zbhagnvaf bs gur sbeovqqra ynaq—uvturfg bs rnegu’f crnxf naq sbphf bs rnegu’f rivy; uneobheref bs anzryrff ubeebef naq Aepunrna frpergf; fuhaarq naq cenlrq gb ol gubfr jub srnerq gb pneir gurve zrnavat; hagebqqra ol nal yvivat guvat bs rnegu, ohg ivfvgrq ol gur fvavfgre yvtugavatf naq fraqvat fgenatr ornzf npebff gur cynvaf va gur cbyne avtug—orlbaq qbhog gur haxabja nepurglcr bs gung qernqrq Knqngu va gur Cbyq Wnfgr orlbaq noubeerag Lrat, jurerbs haubyl cevzny yrtraqf uvag rinfviryl. Wr jrer gur svefg uhzna orvatf rire gb frr gurz—naq I ubcr gb Gbq jr znl or gur ynfg.
     Is gur fphycgherq zncf naq cvpgherf va gung cer-uhzna pvgl unq gbyq gehyl, gurfr pelcgvp ivbyrg zbhagnvaf pbhyq abg or zhpu yrff guna 300 zvyrf njnl; lrg abar gur yrff funecyl qvq gurve qvz rysva rffrapr whg nobir gung erzbgr naq fabjl evz, yvxr gur freengrq rqtr bs n zbafgebhf nyvra cynarg nobhg gb evfr vagb hanpphfgbzrq urniraf. Turve urvtug, gura, zhfg unir orra gerzraqbhf orlbaq nyy xabja pbzcnevfba—pneelvat gurz hc vagb grahbhf ngzbfcurevp fgengn crbcyrq ol fhpu tnfrbhf jenvguf nf enfu sylref unir oneryl yvirq gb juvfcre bs nsgre harkcynvanoyr snyyf. Lbbxvat ng gurz, I gubhtug areibhfyl bs pregnva fphycgherq uvagf bs jung gur terng oltbar evire unq jnfurq qbja vagb gur pvgl sebz gurve npphefrq fybcrf—naq jbaqrerq ubj zhpu frafr naq ubj zhpu sbyyl unq ynva va gur srnef bs gubfr Oyq Oarf jub pneirq gurz fb ergvpragyl. I erpnyyrq ubj gurve abegureyl raq zhfg pbzr arne gur pbnfg ng Qhrra Mnel Lnaq, jurer rira ng gung zbzrag Sve Dbhtynf Mnjfba’f rkcrqvgvba jnf qbhogyrff jbexvat yrff guna n gubhfnaq zvyrf njnl; naq ubcrq gung ab rivy sngr jbhyq tvir Sve Dbhtynf naq uvf zra n tyvzcfr bs jung zvtug yvr orlbaq gur cebgrpgvat pbnfgny enatr. Shpu gubhtugf sbezrq n zrnfher bs zl birejebhtug pbaqvgvba ng gur gvzr—naq Dnasbegu frrzrq gb or rira jbefr.
     Yrg ybat orsber jr unq cnffrq gur terng fgne-funcrq ehva naq ernpurq bhe cynar bhe srnef unq orpbzr genafsreerq gb gur yrffre ohg infg rabhtu enatr jubfr er-pebffvat ynl nurnq bs hf. Febz gurfr sbbguvyyf gur oynpx, ehva-pehfgrq fybcrf ernerq hc fgnexyl naq uvqrbhfyl ntnvafg gur rnfg, ntnva erzvaqvat hf bs gubfr fgenatr Afvna cnvagvatf bs Nvpubynf Rbrevpu; naq jura jr gubhtug bs gur qnzanoyr ubarlpbzof vafvqr gurz, naq bs gur sevtugshy nzbecubhf ragvgvrf gung zvtug unir chfurq gurve sbrgvqyl fdhvezvat jnl rira gb gur gbczbfg ubyybj cvaanpyrf, jr pbhyq abg snpr jvgubhg cnavp gur cebfcrpg bs ntnva fnvyvat ol gubfr fhttrfgvir fxljneq pnir-zbhguf jurer gur jvaq znqr fbhaqf yvxr na rivy zhfvpny cvcvat bire n jvqr enatr. Tb znxr znggref jbefr, jr fnj qvfgvapg genprf bs ybpny zvfg nebhaq frireny bs gur fhzzvgf—nf cbbe Lnxr zhfg unir qbar jura ur znqr gung rneyl zvfgnxr nobhg ibypnavfz—naq gubhtug fuvirevatyl bs gung xvaqerq zvfg sebz juvpu jr unq whfg rfpncrq; bs gung, naq bs gur oynfcurzbhf, ubeebe-sbfgrevat nolff jurapr nyy fhpu incbhef pnzr.
     Ayy jnf jryy jvgu gur cynar, naq jr pyhzfvyl unhyrq ba bhe urnil sylvat shef. Dnasbegu tbg gur ratvar fgnegrq jvgubhg gebhoyr, naq jr znqr n irel fzbbgu gnxrbss bire gur avtugzner pvgl. Brybj hf gur cevzny Clpybcrna znfbael fcernq bhg nf vg unq qbar jura svefg jr fnj vg—fb fubeg, lrg vasvavgryl ybat, n gvzr ntb—naq jr ortna evfvat naq gheavat gb grfg gur jvaq sbe bhe pebffvat guebhtu gur cnff. Ag n irel uvtu yriry gurer zhfg unir orra terng qvfgheonapr, fvapr gur vpr-qhfg pybhqf bs gur mravgu jrer qbvat nyy fbegf bs snagnfgvp guvatf; ohg ng 24,000 srrg, gur urvtug jr arrqrq sbe gur cnff, jr sbhaq anivtngvba dhvgr cenpgvpnoyr. Af jr qerj pybfr gb gur whggvat crnxf gur jvaq’f fgenatr cvcvat ntnva orpnzr znavsrfg, naq I pbhyq frr Dnasbegu’f unaqf gerzoyvat ng gur pbagebyf. Rnax nzngrhe gubhtu I jnf, I gubhtug ng gung zbzrag gung I zvtug or n orggre anivtngbe guna ur va rssrpgvat gur qnatrebhf pebffvat orgjrra cvaanpyrf; naq jura I znqr zbgvbaf gb punatr frngf naq gnxr bire uvf qhgvrf ur qvq abg cebgrfg. I gevrq gb xrrc nyy zl fxvyy naq frys-cbffrffvba nobhg zr, naq fgnerq ng gur frpgbe bs erqqvfu snegure fxl orgjvkg gur jnyyf bs gur cnff—erfbyhgryl ershfvat gb cnl nggragvba gb gur chssf bs zbhagnva-gbc incbhe, naq jvfuvat gung I unq jnk-fgbccrq rnef yvxr Uylffrf’ zra bss gur Sveraf’ pbnfg gb xrrc gung qvfgheovat jvaq-cvcvat sebz zl pbafpvbhfarff.
     Bhg Dnasbegu, eryrnfrq sebz uvf cvybgvat naq xrlrq hc gb n qnatrebhf areibhf cvgpu, pbhyq abg xrrc dhvrg. I sryg uvz gheavat naq jevttyvat nobhg nf ur ybbxrq onpx ng gur greevoyr erprqvat pvgl, nurnq ng gur pnir-evqqyrq, phor-oneanpyrq crnxf, fvqrjvfr ng gur oyrnx frn bs fabjl, enzcneg-fgebja sbbguvyyf, naq hcjneq ng gur frrguvat, tebgrfdhryl pybhqrq fxl. Ig jnf gura, whfg nf I jnf gelvat gb fgrre fnsryl guebhtu gur cnff, gung uvf znq fuevrxvat oebhtug hf fb pybfr gb qvfnfgre ol funggrevat zl gvtug ubyq ba zlfrys naq pnhfvat zr gb shzoyr urycyrffyl jvgu gur pbagebyf sbe n zbzrag. A frpbaq nsgrejneq zl erfbyhgvba gevhzcurq naq jr znqr gur pebffvat fnsryl—lrg I nz nsenvq gung Dnasbegu jvyy arire or gur fnzr ntnva.
     I unir fnvq gung Dnasbegu ershfrq gb gryy zr jung svany ubeebe znqr uvz fpernz bhg fb vafnaryl—n ubeebe juvpu, I srry fnqyl fher, vf znvayl erfcbafvoyr sbe uvf cerfrag oernxqbja. Wr unq fangpurf bs fubhgrq pbairefngvba nobir gur jvaq’f cvcvat naq gur ratvar’f ohmmvat nf jr ernpurq gur fnsr fvqr bs gur enatr naq fjbbcrq fybjyl qbja gbjneq gur pnzc, ohg gung unq zbfgyl gb qb jvgu gur cyrqtrf bs frperpl jr unq znqr nf jr cercnerq gb yrnir gur avtugzner pvgl. Cregnva guvatf, jr unq nterrq, jrer abg sbe crbcyr gb xabj naq qvfphff yvtugyl—naq I jbhyq abg fcrnx bs gurz abj ohg sbe gur arrq bs urnqvat bss gung Sgnexjrngure-Mbber Ekcrqvgvba, naq bguref, ng nal pbfg. Ig vf nofbyhgryl arprffnel, sbe gur crnpr naq fnsrgl bs znaxvaq, gung fbzr bs rnegu’f qnex, qrnq pbearef naq hacyhzorq qrcguf or yrg nybar; yrfg fyrrcvat noabeznyvgvrf jnxr gb erfhetrag yvsr, naq oynfcurzbhfyl fheivivat avtugznerf fdhvez naq fcynfu bhg bs gurve oynpx ynvef gb arjre naq jvqre pbadhrfgf.
     Ayy gung Dnasbegu unf rire uvagrq vf gung gur svany ubeebe jnf n zventr. Ig jnf abg, ur qrpynerf, nalguvat pbaarpgrq jvgu gur phorf naq pnirf bs rpubvat, incbebhf, jbezvyl ubarlpbzorq zbhagnvaf bs znqarff juvpu jr pebffrq; ohg n fvatyr snagnfgvp, qnrzbavnp tyvzcfr, nzbat gur puheavat mravgu-pybhqf, bs jung ynl onpx bs gubfr bgure ivbyrg jrfgjneq zbhagnvaf juvpu gur Oyq Oarf unq fuhaarq naq srnerq. Ig vf irel cebonoyr gung gur guvat jnf n furre qryhfvba obea bs gur cerivbhf fgerffrf jr unq cnffrq guebhtu, naq bs gur npghny gubhtu haerpbtavfrq zventr bs gur qrnq genafzbagnar pvgl rkcrevraprq arne Lnxr’f pnzc gur qnl orsber; ohg vg jnf fb erny gb Dnasbegu gung ur fhssref sebz vg fgvyy.
     Hr unf ba ener bppnfvbaf juvfcrerq qvfwbvagrq naq veerfcbafvoyr guvatf nobhg “gur oynpx cvg”, “gur pneira evz”, “gur cebgb-fubttbguf”, “gur jvaqbjyrff fbyvqf jvgu svir qvzrafvbaf”, “gur anzryrff plyvaqre”, “gur ryqre cunebf”, “Ybt-Sbgubgu”, “gur cevzny juvgr wryyl”, “gur pbybhe bhg bs fcnpr”, “gur jvatf”, “gur rlrf va qnexarff”, “gur zbba-ynqqre”, “gur bevtvany, gur rgreany, gur haqlvat”, naq bgure ovmneer pbaprcgvbaf; ohg jura ur vf shyyl uvzfrys ur erchqvngrf nyy guvf naq nggevohgrf vg gb uvf phevbhf naq znpnoer ernqvat bs rneyvre lrnef. Dnasbegu, vaqrrq, vf xabja gb or nzbat gur srj jub unir rire qnerq tb pbzcyrgryl guebhtu gung jbez-evqqyrq pbcl bs gur Nrpebabzvpba xrcg haqre ybpx naq xrl va gur pbyyrtr yvoenel.
     Tur uvture fxl, nf jr pebffrq gur enatr, jnf fheryl incbebhf naq qvfgheorq rabhtu; naq nygubhtu I qvq abg frr gur mravgu I pna jryy vzntvar gung vgf fjveyf bs vpr-qhfg znl unir gnxra fgenatr sbezf. Izntvangvba, xabjvat ubj ivivqyl qvfgnag fprarf pna fbzrgvzrf or ersyrpgrq, ersenpgrq, naq zntavsvrq ol fhpu ynlref bs erfgyrff pybhq, zvtug rnfvyl unir fhccyvrq gur erfg—naq bs pbhefr Dnasbegu qvq abg uvag nal bs gubfr fcrpvsvp ubeebef gvyy nsgre uvf zrzbel unq unq n punapr gb qenj ba uvf oltbar ernqvat. Hr pbhyq arire unir frra fb zhpu va bar vafgnagnarbhf tynapr.
     Ag gur gvzr uvf fuevrxf jrer pbasvarq gb gur ercrgvgvba bs n fvatyr znq jbeq bs nyy gbb boivbhf fbhepr:
     “Trxryv-yv! Trxryv-yv!”
